brahmacariyavāso nāma idha maggabrahmacariyassa nibbattanamevāti āha nti sammādiṭṭhiyā  catūsu saccesu pariññādikiccasādhanavasena pavattamānāya sammā saṅkappādīnampi dukkhasacce pariññābhisamayānuguṇā pavatti itarasaccesu ca nesaṃ pahānābhisamayādivasena pavatti pākaṭā eva tena vuttaṃ ti ti ime pakārā itthaṃ tabbhāvo itthattaṃ tadatthanti vuttaṃ  hoti te pana pakārā ariyamaggabyāpārabhūtā pariññādayo idhādhippetāti āha ti te hi maggaṃ paccavekkhato maggānubhāvena pākaṭā hutvā upaṭṭhahanti pariññādīsu ca pahānameva padhānaṃ tadatthattā itaresanti āha ti pahīnakilesapaccavekkhaṇavasena vā etaṃ vuttaṃ ti nissakke sampadānavacananti āha ti  anāgataṃ  carimattabhāvasaṅkhātā  ti etena tesaṃ appatiṭṭhataṃ dasseti apariññāmūlakā hi patiṭṭhā yathāha kabaḷīkāre ce bhikkhave āhāre atthi rāgo atthi nandī atthi taṇhā patiṭṭhitaṃ tattha viññāṇaṃ virūḷhantiādi  tenevāha tiādi
 na paṭhamadutiyañāṇadvayādhigamaṃ viya kevalanti adhippāyo  nigamanavasenāti adhippāyo sarūpato hi taṃ pubbe dassitamevāti pubbenivāsañāṇena atītārammaṇasabhāgatāya tabbhāvībhāvato ca atītaṃsañāṇaṃ saṅgahetvāti yojanā tattha nti atītakhandhāyatanadhātusaṅkhāte atītakoṭṭhāse appaṭihataṃ ñāṇaṃ ti saparibhaṇḍena dibbacakkhuñāṇena paccuppannaṃso ca anāgataṃso ca paccuppannānāgataṃsaṃ tattha ñāṇaṃ nti etena sabbaṃ lokaṃ uttaritvā abhibhuyya ṭhitattā sabbaññutaññāṇassa viya sesāsādhāraṇañāṇassa balañāṇaāveṇikabuddhadhammādīnampi anaññasādhāraṇānaṃ buddhaguṇānaṃ saṅgaho veditabbo tenāha ti


ti ettha ti appevāti iminā samānattho nipāto  tasmā brāhmaṇa appeva kho pana te evamassāti  attho yaṃ pana ti vuttaṃ tampi imamevatthaṃ sandhāya vuttaṃ akāraṇaṃ brāhmaṇena parikappitamatthaṃ paṭipakkhipitvā attano adhippetaṃ kāraṇaṃ dassento atthova phalaṃ tadadhīnavuttitāya vaso etassāti  hetūti evaṃ vā ettha attho daṭṭhabbo nti etena satthā attano vivekābhiratiṃ pakāsetīti dassento tiādimāha tattha nti iriyāpathapavattīnaṃ tappavattiyo hi ekasmiṃ iriyāpathe uppannadukkhaṃ aññena iriyāpathena vicchinditvā haraṇato vihārāti vuccanti ti etena yo ādito brāhmaṇena bhavaṃ tesaṃ gotamo pubbaṅgamo diṭṭhānugatiṃ āpajjatīti vutto yo ca tathā evametaṃ brāhmaṇātiādinā attanā sampaṭicchito tameva atthaṃ nigamanavasena dassento yathānusandhināva satthā desanaṃ niṭṭhāpesi


 evaṃ niṭṭhāpitāya desanāya brāhmaṇo tattha bhagavati pasādaṃ pavedento ntiādimāha ti  atikkantā vigatāti atthoti āha ti teneva hi ti vuttaṃ ti ativiya kantataro manoramo tādiso ca sundaro bhaddako nāma hotīti āha ti
ti devanāgayakkhagandhabbādīsu ko katamo ti mama ti pāde ti imāya evarūpāya deviddhiyā ti iminā edisena parivārena parijanena nti vijjotamāno ti ativiya kantena kamanīyena abhirūpena ti chavivaṇṇena sarīravaṇṇanibhāya ti dasapi disā obhāsento pabhāsento cando viya sūriyo viya ca ekobhāsaṃ ekālokaṃ  karontoti gāthāya attho ti uḷārarūpe sampannarūpe
coro  coro sappo sappotiādīsu  vijjha vijjha pahara paharātiādīsu  sādhu sādhūtiādīsu   gaccha gaccha lunāhi lunāhītiādīsu  āgaccha āgacchātiādīsu  buddho buddhoti cintentotiādīsu   abhikkamathāyasmanto abhikkamathāyasmantotiādīsu   kahaṃ ekaputtaka kahaṃ ekaputtakātiādīsu   aho sukhaṃ aho sukhantiādīsu   -saddo avuttasamuccayattho tena garahāasammānādīnaṃ saṅgaho daṭṭhabbo tattha pāpo pāpotiādīsu  abhirūpaka abhirūpakātiādīsu  daṭṭhabbaṃ
nayidaṃ āmeḍitavasena dvikkhattuṃ vuttaṃ atha kho atthadvayavasenāti dassento tiādimāha nti vacanaṃ apekkhitvā napuṃsakaliṅgavasena vuttaṃ taṃ pana bhagavato vacanaṃ dhammassa desanāti katvā tathā vuttaṃ atthamattadassanaṃ vā etaṃ tasmā atthavasena liṅgavibhattivipariṇāmo veditabbo dutiyapadepi eseva nayo ti rāgādikilesadosavidhamanato ti sīlādiguṇānaṃ sampāpanato ye guṇe desanā adhigameti tesu padhānabhūtā dassetabbāti te padhānabhūte tāva dassetuṃ ti vuttaṃ saddhāpamukhā hi lokiyā guṇā paññāpamukhā lokuttarā sīlādiatthasampattiyā  sabhāvaniruttisampattiyā  suviññeyyasaddapayogatāya  saṇhasukhumabhāvena dubbiññeyyatthatāya  siniddhamudumadhurasaddapayogatāya  vipulavisuddhapemanīyatthatāya  mānātimānavidhamanena  thambhasārambhamaddanena  hitādhippāyapavattiyā paresaṃ rāgapariḷāhādivūpasamanena ca  kilesandhakāravidhamanena  karavīkarutamañjutāya  pubbāparāviruddhasuvisuddhatthatāya  āpātharamaṇīyatāya eva  vimaddakkhamatāya hitajjhāsayappavattitatāya ca ti saddena saṃsāracakkanivattanato saddhammacakkappavattanato micchāvādavidhamanato sammāvādapatiṭṭhāpanato akusalamūlasamuddharaṇato kusalamūlasaṃropanato apāyadvārapidhānato saggamaggadvāravivaraṇato pariyuṭṭhānavūpasamanato anusayasamugghātanatoti evamādīnaṃ saṅgaho daṭṭhabbo
nti  kenaci adhomukhaṃ ṭhapitaṃ nti sabhāveneva heṭṭhāmukhajātaṃ ti vivaṭaṃ kareyya ti puratthābhimukho uttarābhimukho vā gacchātiādīni avatvā hatthe gahetvā nissandehaṃ esa maggo evaṃ gacchāti vadeyya ti kāḷapakkhe cātuddasī
 ādheyyassa anādhārabhūtaṃ bhājanaṃ ādhārabhāvāpādanavasena  heṭṭhāmukhajātatāya  adhomukhaṭṭhapitatāya nti evaṃ padadvayaṃ yathārahaṃ yojetabbaṃ na yathāsaṅkhyaṃ kāmaṃ kāmacchandādayopi paṭicchādakā micchādiṭṭhi pana savisesaṃ paṭicchādikāti āha nti tenāha bhagavā micchādiṭṭhiparamāhaṃ bhikkhave vajjaṃ vadāmīti  sabbo apāyagāmimaggo  kucchito maggoti katvā sammādiṭṭhiādīnaṃ ujupaṭipakkhatāya micchādiṭṭhiādayo aṭṭha micchattadhammā  teneva hi tadubhayapaṭipakkhataṃ sandhāya ti vuttaṃ sappiādisannissayo padīpo na tathā ujjalo yathā telasannissayoti  ti etehi nikujjitukkujjanapaṭicchannavivaraṇādiupamopamitabbapakārehi  vā yathāvuttehi soḷasārammaṇapariggahaasammohavihāradibbavihāravibhāvanapariyāyehi vijjāttayavibhāvanāpadesena attano sabbaññuguṇavibhāvanapariyāyehi ca tenāha ti


nti  pasannehi kātabbaṃ sakkāraṃ nti paṭisaraṇaṃ tenāha nti parāyaṇabhāvo ca anatthanisedhanena atthasampaṭipādanena ca hotīti āha ti ti dukkhatoti vadanti pāpatoti pana yuttaṃ nissakke cetaṃ sāmivacanaṃ ettha ca nāyaṃ gami-saddo nī-saddādayo viya dvikammako tasmā yathā ajaṃ gāmaṃ netīti vuccati evaṃ gotamaṃ saraṇaṃ gacchāmīti vattuṃ na sakkā saraṇanti gacchāmīti pana vattabbaṃ iti-saddo cettha luttaniddiṭṭho tassa cāyamattho  gamanañca tadadhippāyena bhajanaṃ tathā jānanaṃ vāti dassento tiādimāha  tattha tiādīsu purimassa purimassa pacchimaṃ pacchimaṃ atthavacanaṃ  vā saraṇādhippāyena upasaṅkamanaṃ  santikāvacaratā  vattapaṭivattakaraṇena upaṭṭhānanti evaṃ sabbathāpi anaññasaraṇataṃyeva dīpeti ti padassa kathaṃ bujjhāmīti ayamattho labbhatīti āha tiādi
ti padadvayenapi phalaṭṭhā eva dassitā na maggaṭṭhāti te dassento ti āha nanu ca kalyāṇaputhujjanopi yathānusiṭṭhaṃ paṭipajjatīti vuccatīti kiñcāpi vuccati nippariyāyena pana maggaṭṭhā eva tathā vattabbā na itare niyāmokkamanābhāvato tathā hi te eva ti vuttā sammattaniyāmokkamanena hi apāyavinimuttisambhavo ti ettha -saddo ādiattho pakārattho vā tena yāvatā bhikkhave dhammā saṅkhatā vā asaṅkhatā vā virāgo tesaṃ aggamakkhāyatīti   saṅgaṇhāti ti vā iminā ettha ca  niyyānikatāya  tassa tadatthasiddhihetutāyāti ubhayamevettha nippariyāyena dhammoti vutto nibbānañhi ārammaṇapaccayabhūtaṃ labhitvā ariyamaggassa tadatthasiddhi ariyaphalānaṃ yasmā tāya saddhāya avūpasantāyātiādivacanato maggena samucchinnānaṃ kilesānaṃ paṭippassaddhipahānakiccatāya niyyānānuguṇatāya niyyānapariyosānatāya ca pariyattidhammassa pana niyyānadhammasamadhigamahetutāyāti iminā  pariyāyena dhammabhāvo labbhati eva svāyamattho pāṭhāruḷho evāti dassento na kevalantiādimāha
kāmarāgo bhavarāgoti evamādibhedo sabbopi rāgo virajjati pahīyati etenāti  ejāsaṅkhātāya taṇhāya antonijjhānalakkhaṇassa sokassa ca taduppattiyaṃ sabbaso parikkhīṇattā nti avirodhadīpanato kenaci aviruddhaṃ iṭṭhaṃ paṇītanti vā attho paguṇarūpena pavattitattā pakaṭṭhaguṇavibhāvanato vā  yathāha vihiṃsasaññī paguṇaṃ na bhāsiṃ dhammaṃ paṇītaṃ manujesu brahmeti sabbadhammakkhandhā kathitāti yojanā
ti yāyaṃ diṭṭhi ariyā niyyānikā niyyāti takkarassa sammā dukkhakkhayāya tathārūpāya diṭṭhiyā diṭṭhisāmaññagato viharatīti  evaṃ vuttāya diṭṭhiyā yāni tāni sīlāni akhaṇḍāni acchiddāni asabalāni akammāsāni bhujissāni viññuppasatthāni aparāmaṭṭhāni samādhisaṃvattanikāni  tathārūpehi sīlehi sīlasāmaññagato viharatīti  evaṃ vuttānaṃ sīlānañca saṃhatabhāvena diṭṭhisīlasāmaññenāti attho ti ghaṭito ariyapuggalā hi yattha katthaci dūre ṭhitāpi attano guṇasāmaggiyā saṃhatā eva ti te purisayugavasena cattāropi puggalavasena aṭṭheva ariyadhammassa paccakkhadassāvitāya dhammadasā tīṇi vatthūni saraṇanti gamanena tikkhattuṃ gamanena ca  ti attano hadayagataṃ vācāya pavedesi


saraṇagamanassa visayapabhedaphalasaṃkilesabhedānaṃ viya kattu ca vibhāvanā tattha kosallāya hotīti ti vuttaṃ tena vinā saraṇagamanasseva asambhavato kasmā panettha vodānaṃ na gahitaṃ nanu vodānavibhāvanāpi tattha kosallāvahāti saccametaṃ taṃ pana saṃkilesaggahaṇeneva atthato dīpitaṃ hotīti na gahitaṃ yāni hi tesaṃ saṃkilesakāraṇāni aññāṇādīni tesaṃ sabbena sabbaṃ anuppannānaṃ anuppādanena uppannānañca pahānena vodānaṃ hotīti hiṃsatthassa sara-saddassa vasenetaṃ padaṃ daṭṭhabbanti nti vatvā taṃ pana hiṃsanaṃ kesaṃ kathaṃ kassa vāti codanaṃ sodhento ntiādimāha tattha nti vaṭṭabhayaṃ nti cittutrāsaṃ teneva cetasikadukkhassa gahitattā nti idha kāyikaṃ dukkhaṃ nti duggatipariyāpannaṃ sabbaṃ dukkhaṃ tayidaṃ sabbaṃ parato phalakathāyaṃ āvi bhavissati nti saraṇanti padaṃ
evaṃ avisesato saraṇasaddassa atthaṃ dassetvā idāni visesato dassetuṃ tiādi vuttaṃ ti sampannasīlā bhikkhave viharathātiādinā  atthe niyojanena ti ntiādinā ādīnavadassanādimukhena anatthato vinivattanena ti hitāhitesu appavattipavattihetukaṃ byasanaṃ appavattikaraṇena vināseti   maggasaṅkhāto dhammo itaro  sattānaṃ bhayaṃ hiṃsatīti yojanā nti dānavasena pūjāvasena ca upanītānaṃ sakkārānaṃ  sattānaṃ bhayaṃ hiṃsati anuttaradakkhiṇeyyabhāvatoti adhippāyo ti imināpi vibhajitvā vuttena kāraṇena
sammāsambuddho bhagavā svākkhāto dhammo suppaṭipanno saṅghoti evaṃ pavatto tattha ratanattaye pasādo tappasādo tadeva ratanattayaṃ garu etassāti taggaru tassa bhāvo taggarutā tappasādo ca taggarutā ca  tāhi vidhutadiṭṭhivicikicchāsammohaassaddhiyāditāya  tadeva ratanattayaṃ parāyaṇaṃ gati  tāṇaṃ leṇanti evaṃ ākārena pavattiyā  saraṇanti gacchati etenāti ti tena yathāvuttacittuppādena samannāgato ti evaṃ bhajati sevati payirupāsati evaṃ vā jānāti bujjhatīti evamattho veditabbo ettha ca pasādaggahaṇena lokiyasaraṇagamanamāha tañhi pasādappadhānaṃ na ñāṇappadhānaṃ garutāgahaṇena lokuttaraṃ ariyā hi ratanattayaṃ guṇābhiññātāya pāsāṇacchattaṃ viya garuṃ katvā passanti tasmā tappasādena vikkhambhanavasena vihatakileso taggarutāya samucchedavasenāti yojetabbaṃ tapparāyaṇatā panettha taggatikatāti tāya catubbidhampi vakkhamānaṃ saraṇagamanaṃ gahitanti daṭṭhabbaṃ avisesena vā pasādagarutā jotitāti pasādaggahaṇena aveccappasādassa itarassa ca gahaṇaṃ tathā garutāgahaṇenāti ubhayenapi ubhayaṃ saraṇagamanaṃ yojetabbaṃ
maggakkhaṇe ijjhatīti yojanā ti etena atthato catusaccādhigamoyeva lokuttaraṃ saraṇagamananti dasseti tattha hi nibbānadhammo sacchikiriyābhisamayavasena maggadhammo bhāvanābhisamayavasena paṭivijjhiyamānoyeva saraṇagamanattaṃ sādheti buddhaguṇā pana sāvakagocarabhūtā pariññābhisamayavasena tathā ariyasaṅghaguṇā tenāha ti ijjhantañca saheva ijjhati na lokiyaṃ viya paṭipāṭiyā asammohapaṭivedhena paṭividdhattāti adhippāyo ye pana vadanti na saraṇagamanaṃ nibbānārammaṇaṃ hutvā pavattati maggassa adhigatattā pana adhigatameva hoti ekaccānaṃ tevijjādīnaṃ lokiyavijjādayo viyāti tesaṃ lokiyameva saraṇagamanaṃ siyā na lokuttaraṃ tañca ayuttaṃ duvidhassapi icchitabbattā nti lokiyasaraṇagamanaṃ  sammāsambuddho bhagavātiādinā ti yathāvuttasaddhāpubbaṅgamā  buddhasubuddhataṃ dhammasudhammataṃ saṅghasuppaṭipatiñca lokiyāvabodhavaseneva  sammā ñāyena dassanato saddhāmūlikā sammādiṭṭhīti etena saddhūpanissayā yathāvuttalakkhaṇā paññā lokiyasaraṇagamananti dasseti tenāha ti diṭṭhi eva attano paccayehi ujuṃ karīyatīti katvā diṭṭhi vā ujuṃ karīyati etenāti  tathā pavatto cittuppādo  evañca katvā tapparāyaṇatākārapavatto cittuppādoti idañca vacanaṃ samatthitaṃ hoti saddhāpubbaṅgamasammādiṭṭhiggahaṇaṃ pana cittuppādassa tappadhānatāyāti daṭṭhabbaṃ saddhāpaṭilābhoti iminā mātādīhi ussāhitadārakādīnaṃ viya ñāṇavippayuttasaraṇagamanaṃ dasseti sammādiṭṭhīti iminā ñāṇasampayuttasaraṇagamanaṃ
 lokiyaṃ saraṇagamanaṃ  sanniyyātīyati appīyati pariccajīyati etenāti  yathāvuttaṃ diṭṭhijukammaṃ taṃ ratanattayaṃ parāyaṇaṃ paṭisaraṇaṃ etassāti tapparāyaṇo puggalo cittuppādo vā tassa bhāvo  yathāvuttadiṭṭhijukammameva saraṇanti adhippāyena sissabhāvaṃ antevāsikabhāvaṃ upagacchati etenāti  saraṇagamanādhippāyeneva paṇipatati etenāti  sabbattha yathāvuttadiṭṭhijukammavaseneva attho veditabbo nti saṃsāradukkhanittharaṇatthaṃ attano attabhāvassa pariccajanaṃ esa nayo sesesupi ti avadhāraṇaṃ itaresupi saraṇagamanavisesesu yathārahaṃ vattabbaṃ evañhi tadaññanivattanaṃ kataṃ hoti
evaṃ attasanniyātanādīni ekena pakārena dassetvā idāni aparehipi pakārehi dassetuṃ tiādi āraddhaṃ tena pariyāyantarehipi attasanniyyātanādi katameva hoti atthassa abhinnattāti dasseti nti -saddena sātāgirihemavatādīnaṃ saṅgaho daṭṭhabbo nanu cete āḷavakādayo maggeneva āgatasaraṇagamanā kathaṃ tesaṃ tapparāyaṇatāsaraṇagamanaṃ vuttanti maggenāgatasaraṇagamanehipi so ahaṃ vicarissāmi gāmā gāmantiādinā  tehi tapparāyaṇatākārassa paveditattā tathā vuttaṃ
ti ettha ñātivasena bhayavasena ācariyavasena dakkhiṇeyyavasenāti paccekaṃ vasenāti padaṃ yojetabbaṃ tattha ti ñātibhāvavasena evaṃ sesesupi ti dakkhiṇeyyatāhetukena paṇipātena ti ñātibhāvādivasappavattehi tīhi paṇipātehi tiādinā saṅkhepato  vuttamatthaṃ vitthārato dassetuṃ tiādi vuttaṃ ti paṇipātassa lakkhaṇavacanaṃ nti diṭṭhadhammikaṃ  sandhāya vadati samparāyikañhi niyyānikaṃ vā anusāsanaṃ paccāsīsanto dakkhiṇeyyapaṇipātameva karotīti adhippāyo ti saraṇagamanavibhāgo
ariyamaggoyeva lokuttarasaraṇagamananti āha nti ti sakalassa vaṭṭadukkhassa anuppādanirodho nti cattāri ariyasaccāni sammappaññāya passatīti  evaṃ vuttaṃ ariyasaccadassanaṃ
ti niccanti aggahaṇādivasena nti hetupaṭikkhepo ti paccayapaṭikkhepo ubhayenapi kāraṇameva paṭikkhipati nti yena kāraṇena ti maggadiṭṭhiyā sampanno sotāpanno nti catubhūmakesu saṅkhatasaṅkhāresu ekasaṅkhārampi ti niccoti gaṇheyya ti ekantasukhī attā hoti arogo paraṃ maraṇāti  evaṃ attadiṭṭhivasena sukhato gāhaṃ sandhāyetaṃ vuttaṃ diṭṭhivippayuttacittena pana ariyasāvako pariḷāhavūpasamanatthaṃ mattahatthiparittāsito viya cokkhabrāhmaṇo ukkārabhūmiṃ kañci saṅkhāraṃ sukhato upagacchati attavāre kasiṇādipaññattisaṅgahaṇatthaṃ saṅkhāranti avatvā nti vuttaṃ imesupi vāresu catubhūmakavaseneva paricchedo veditabbo tebhūmakavaseneva vā yaṃ yañhi puthujjano gāhavasena gaṇhāti tato tato ariyasāvako gāhaṃ viniveṭheti ntiādīsu janikā mātā janako pitā manussabhūto khīṇāsavo ti adhippeto kiṃ pana ariyasāvako aññaṃ jīvitā voropeyyāti etampi aṭṭhānaṃ puthujjanabhāvassa pana mahāsāvajjabhāvadassanatthaṃ ariyasāvakassa phaladīpanatthañcevaṃ vuttaṃ  vadhakacittena paduṭṭhacitto ti jīvamānakasarīre khuddakamakkhikāya pivanamattampi lohitaṃ uppādeyya ti samānasaṃvāsakaṃ samānasīmāyaṃ ṭhitaṃ saṅghaṃ kammena uddesena voharanto anussāvanena salākaggāhenāti  evaṃ vuttehi pañcahi kāraṇehi bhindeyya  nti aññaṃ titthakaraṃ ayaṃ me satthāti evaṃ gaṇheyyāti ti attho
nti te buddhaṃ saraṇaṃ gatā tannimittaṃ apāyabhūmiṃ na gamissanti  pana ti attho
ti dasahi kāraṇehi ti adhibhavanti ti ettha caturāsītisahassasaṅkhānaṃ suvaṇṇapātirūpiyapātikaṃsapātīnaṃ yathākkamaṃ rūpiyasuvaṇṇahiraññapūrānaṃ karīsassa catutthabhāvappamāṇānaṃ sabbālaṅkārapaṭimaṇḍitānaṃ caturāsītiyā hatthisahassānaṃ caturāsītiyā assasahassānaṃ caturāsītiyā rathasahassānaṃ caturāsītiyā dhenusahassānaṃ caturāsītiyā kaññāsahassānaṃ caturāsītiyā pallaṅkasahassānaṃ caturāsītiyā vatthakoṭisahassānaṃ aparimāṇassa ca khajjabhojjādibhedassa āhārassa pariccajanavasena sattamāsādhikāni satta saṃvaccharāni nirantaraṃ pavattavelāmamahādānato ekassa sotāpannassa dinnadānaṃ mahapphalataraṃ tato sataṃ sotāpannānaṃ dinnadānato ekassa sakadāgāmissa tato ekassa anāgāmissa tato ekassa arahato tato ekassa paccekabuddhassa tato sammāsambuddhassa tato buddhappamukhassa saṅghassa dinnadānaṃ mahapphalataraṃ tato cātuddisaṃ saṅghaṃ uddissa vihārakaraṇaṃ tato saraṇagamanaṃ mahapphalataranti imamatthaṃ dīpentassa velāmasuttassa  vasena vuttañhetaṃ yaṃ gahapati velāmo brāhmaṇo dānaṃ adāsi mahādānaṃ yo ekaṃ diṭṭhisampannaṃ bhojeyya idaṃ tato mahapphalatarantiādi  ti -saddena aggappasādasuttādīnaṃ  saṅgaho daṭṭhabbo
 vatthuttayassa guṇānaṃ ajānanaṃ tattha sammoho buddho nu kho na nu kho buddhotiādinā vicikicchā  tassa guṇānaṃ aguṇabhāvaparikappanena viparītaggāho -saddena anādarāgāravādīnaṃ saṅgaho nti na ujjalaṃ aparisuddhaṃ apariyodātanti attho nti anuḷāraṃ ti diṭṭhitaṇhādivasena sadoso lokiyaṃ saraṇagamanaṃ sikkhāsamādānaṃ viya  aggahitakālaparicchedaṃ jīvitapariyantameva hoti tasmā tassa khandhabhedena bhedoti āha ti ti anavajjo saraṇagamanabhedo satipi anavajjatte iṭṭhaphalopi na hotīti āha ti


ti sarūpapucchā tasmā kiṃlakkhaṇo upāsakoti vuttaṃ hoti ti hetupucchā tena kena pavattinimittena upāsakasaddo tasmiṃ puggale niruḷhoti dasseti nti kīdisaṃ assa upāsakassa sīlaṃ kittakena sīlenāyaṃ sīlasampanno nāma hotīti attho ti ko assa sammāājīvo so pana micchājīvassa parivajjanena hotīti sopi vibhajīyatīti ti kā assa sīlassa ājīvassa vā vipatti anantarassa hi vidhi vā paṭisedho vā ti etthāpi eseva nayo
ti khattiyādīsu yo koci tena saraṇagamanamevettha kāraṇaṃ na jātiādivisesoti dasseti ti teneva saraṇagamanena tattha ca sakkaccakāritāya ādaragāravabahumānādiyogena payirupāsanato ti veraṃ vuccati pāṇātipātādidussīlyaṃ tassa maṇanato hananato vināsanato veramaṇiyo pañca viratiyo viratippadhānattā tassa sīlassa tenevāha tattha tattha ti
ti na sammāvaṇijjā ayuttavaṇijjā asāruppavaṇijjā ti akaraṇeneva pajahitvā ti dhammato anapetena tena aññampi adhammikaṃ jīvikaṃ paṭikkhipati ti avisamena tena kāyavisamādiduccaritaṃ vajjetvā kāyasamādinā sucaritena jīvanaṃ dasseti ti āvudhabhaṇḍaṃ katvā vā kāretvā vā yathākataṃ vā paṭilabhitvā tassa vikkayo ti manussavikkayo  ti sūnakārādayo viya migasūkarādike posetvā maṃsaṃ sampādetvā vikkayo ti yaṃ kiñci majjaṃ yojetvā tassa vikkayo ti visaṃ yojetvā visaṃ gahetvā vā tassa vikkayo tattha satthavaṇijjā paroparodhanimittatāya akaraṇīyā vuttā sattavaṇijjā abhujissabhāvakaraṇato maṃsavisavaṇijjā vadhahetuto majjavaṇijjā pamādaṭṭhānato
ti pañcaveramaṇilakkhaṇassa sīlassa ceva pañcamicchāvaṇijjālakkhaṇassa ājīvassa ca ti bhedo pakopo ca ti yāya paṭipattiyā ti upāsakacaṇḍālo nti upāsakamalaṃ ti upāsakanihīno buddhādīsu kammakammaphalesu ca saddhāvipariyāyo assaddhiyaṃ micchādhimokkho yathāvuttena assaddhiyena samannāgato  yathāvutta sīlavipatti ājīvavipattivasena  iminā diṭṭhādinā  idaṃ nāma maṅgalaṃ bhavissatīti evaṃ bālajanaparikappitakotūhalasaṅkhātena diṭṭhasutamutamaṅgalena samannāgato  ti diṭṭhamaṅgalādibhedaṃ maṅgalameva pattiyāyati nti kammassakataṃ no pattiyāyati ti ito sabbaññubuddhasāsanato bahiddhā bāhirakasamaye ti duppaṭipannaṃ dakkhiṇārahasaññī gavesati ti dānamānanādikaṃ kusalakiriyaṃ paṭhamaṃ karoti ettha ca dakkhiṇeyyapariyesanapubbakāre ekaṃ katvā pañca dhammā veditabbā
vipattiyaṃ vuttavipariyāyena  ñātabbā ayaṃ pana viseso  catunnampi parisānaṃ ratijananaṭṭhena upāsakova ratanaṃ  guṇasobhākittisaddasugandhatāhi upāsakova padumaṃ  tathā 
ti ādiatthe nti pariyantakoṭiyaṃ ti ovarakakoṭṭhāsena imasmiṃ gabbhe vasantānaṃ idaṃ nāma panasaphalaṃ pāpuṇātītiādinā taṃtaṃvasanaṭṭhānakoṭṭhāsenāti attho nti ajjaicceva attho
nti iminā tassa saraṇagamanassa āpāṇakoṭikataṃ dassento tiādinā vatvā puna jīvitena taṃ vatthuttayaṃ paṭipūjento saraṇagamanaṃ rakkhāmīti uppannaṃ tassa brāhmaṇassa adhippāyaṃ vibhāvento tiādimāha nti hi yāva me pāṇā dharanti tāva saraṇaṃ upetaṃ upento ca na vācāmattena na ekavāraṃ cittuppādanamattena atha kho pāṇe pariccajitvāpi yāvajīvaṃ upetanti evamettha attho veditabboti



ti ettha -saddo ādiattho evamādikanti attho tena bhikkhū āmantesītiādikaṃ sabbaṃ suttaṃ saṅgaṇhāti tenāha nti tassa ko nikkhepo attajjhāsayo parehi anajjhiṭṭhoyeva hi mahāthero imaṃ desanaṃ ārabhi keci panāhu ekacce bhikkhū saṃkiliṭṭhacitte disvā tesaṃ cittasaṃkilesappahānāya ceva ekaccānaṃ āyatiṃ anuppādanāya ca ayaṃ desanā āraddhāti ti yathā ettha anaṅgaṇasutte evaṃ ito paresūti sabbesupi suttesu anuttānaapubbapadavaṇṇanā eva karīyati tenāha tiādi ti gaṇanena paricchindanaṃ idañhi apparajakkhamahārajakkhatāvasena duvidhe satte paccekaṃ atthaññutānatthaññutāvasena dvidhā katvā cattāroti anavasesapariyādānaṃ vajjīputtakādayo viya puggalavādīti na gahetabbaṃ lokasamaññānusārena atthaṃ paṭivijjhituṃ samatthānaṃ vasena desanāya āraddhattā ayañca desanānayo satthu nissāya evāti dassento tiādimāha

tattha  sammutiyā desanā  paramatthassa desanā  ti sammutiparamatthadesanāsu na sammutiparamatthesu tenāha ti tatridaṃ sammutiparamatthānaṃ lakkhaṇaṃ  yasmiṃ bhinne buddhiyā avayavavinibbhoge vā kate na taṃsamaññā sā ghaṭapaṭādippabhedā sammuti tabbipariyāyato paramattho na hi kakkhaḷaphusanādisabhāve ayaṃ nayo labbhati tattha rūpādidhammaṃ samūhasantānavasena pavattamānaṃ upādāya puggalavohāroti āha ti sesapadesupi eseva nayo uppādavayavanto sabhāvadhammā na niccāti āha ti esa nayo sesapadesupi nanu khandhadesanāpi sammutidesanāva khandhaṭṭho hi rāsaṭṭho koṭṭhāsaṭṭho vāti saccametaṃ ayaṃ pana khandhasamaññā phassādīsu tajjāpaññatti viya paramatthasannissayā tassa āsannatarā puggalasamaññādayo viya na dūreti paramatthasaṅgahatā vuttā khandhasīsena vā tadupādānā sabhāvadhammā eva gahitā nanu ca sabhāvadhammā sabbepi sammutimukheneva desanaṃ ārohanti na samukhenāti sabbāpi desanā sammutidesanāva  siyāti nayidamevaṃ desetabbadhammavibhāgena desanāvibhāgassa adhippetattā na ca saddo kenaci pavattinimittena vinā atthaṃ pakāsetīti
ti idhekacco puggalo attantapo hoti attaparitāpānuyogamanuyuttotiādinā  sammutimukhena pavattitaṃ desanaṃ sutamayañāṇuppādanavasena sutvā ti tadanusārena catusaccasaṅkhātaṃ atthaṃ saha vipassanāya maggena paṭivijjhitvā ti tadekaṭṭhehi kilesehi saddhiṃ anavasesaṃ mohaṃ pajahitvā nti nibbānasaṅkhātaṃ arahattasaṅkhātañca visesaṃ nti tādisānaṃ vineyyānaṃ ti pañcimāni bhikkhave indriyānītiādinā  paramatthadhammavasena sesaṃ anantaranaye vuttasadisameva ti tassaṃ sammutivasena paramatthavasena ca desanāyaṃ ti nānādesabhāsāsu kusalo nti nidassanamattaṃ tiṇṇaṃ vedānaṃ sippaganthānampīti adhippāyo sippuggahaṇañhi parato vakkhati sippāni vā vedantogadhe katvā nti vuttaṃ  na katthaci sannihitabhāvenāti vedānampi kathetabbabhāveneva avaṭṭhānaṃ dīpento guyhā tayī  nihitā gayhatīti micchāvādaṃ paṭikkhipati nānāvidhā desabhāsā etesanti 
paramo uttamo attho  dhammānaṃ yathābhūtasabhāvo lokasaṅketamattasiddhā  yadi evaṃ kathaṃ sammutikathāya saccatātiāha ti lokasamaññaṃ nissāya pavattanato lokasamaññāya hi abhinivesena vinā ñāpanā ekaccassa sutassa sāvanā viya na musā anatidhāvitabbato tassā tenāha bhagavā janapadaniruttiṃ nābhiniveseyya samaññaṃ nātidhāveyyāti  nti sabhāvadhammānaṃ ti yathābhūtasabhāvaṃ nissāya pavattanato ti puggalo sattotiādinā lokasamaññaṃ kathentassa
nti lokapālanakicce hirottappadhamme kiccato pakāsetuṃ tesañhi kiccaṃ sattasantāneyeva pākaṭaṃ hotīti puggalādhiṭṭhānāya kathāya taṃ vattabbaṃ esa nayo sesesupi yasmiñhi cittuppāde kammaṃ uppannaṃ taṃsantāne eva tassa phalassa uppatti  evañhi kataviññāṇanāso akatāgamo vā natthīti sā puggalādhiṭṭhānāya eva kathāya  dīpetabbā tehi sattehi kātabbā puññādikiriyā pi santānavasena nipphādetabbato puggalādhiṭṭhānāya eva kathāya dīpetabbo
nti cutianantaraṃ phalaṃ anantaraṃ nāma tasmiṃ anantare niyuttāni tannibbattanena anantarakaraṇasīlāni anantarapayojanāni vāti  mātughātādīni tesaṃ dīpanatthaṃ tānipi hi santānavasena nipphādetabbato mātaraṃ jīvitā voropetītiādinā  puggalādhiṭṭhānāya eva kathāya dīpetabbāni tathā so mettāsahagatena cetasā ekaṃ disaṃ pharitvā viharatītiādinā  so anekavihitaṃ pubbenivāsaṃ anussarati ekampi jātintiādinā  atthi dakkhiṇā dāyakato visujjhati no paṭiggāhakatotiādinā  ca pavattā  puggalādhiṭṭhānāya eva kathāya dīpetabbā sattasantānavisayattā aṭṭha purisapuggalā  na samayavimutto puggalotiādinā  ca paramatthaṃ kathentopi lokasammutiyā appahānatthaṃ puggalakathaṃ kathesi etena vuttāvasesāya kathāya puggalādhiṭṭhānabhāve payojanaṃ sāmaññavasena saṅgahitanti daṭṭhabbaṃ kāmañcetaṃ sabbaṃ apariññātavatthukānaṃ vasena vuttaṃ pariññātavatthukānampi pana evaṃ desanā sukhāvahā hoti
ti lokiyamahājano  ghanavinibbhogābhāvena dhammakiccassa asallakkhaṇena tattha kiṃ nāmetaṃ kathaṃ nāmetanti saṃsayapakkhandatāya  viruddhābhinivesitāya   ciraparicitatthā vohārakathāya tato eva na  na paṭisattu hoti
 vohāramukhena paramatthassa dīpanato samaññāgahaṇavasena lokena ñāyati samaññāyati voharīyatīti lokasamaññā tāya  tassa tassa atthassa vibhāvane lokena nicchitaṃ niyataṃ vā vuccati voharīyatīti lokanirutti tassaṃ  tathā lokena abhilapīyatīti lokasamaññatāya lokābhilāpo tasmiṃ  appahānato puggalavādino viya 
ti  ettha saddo dīghaṃ santassa yojanantiādīsu  kilantabhāve āgato ayañca vitakko ayañca vicāro santā honti samitātiādīsu  niruddhabhāve āgato adhigato kho myāyaṃ dhammo gambhīro duddaso duranubodho santo paṇītotiādīsu  santañāṇagocaratāya upasantassa sadā satimatotiādīsu  kilesavūpasame santo have sabbhi pavedayantītiādīsu  sādhūsu pañcime bhikkhave mahācorā santo saṃvijjamānātiādīsu  atthibhāve idhāpi atthibhāveyeva so ca puggalasambandhena vuttattā lokasamaññāvasenāti  dassento ti āha ti cetaṃ nipātapadaṃ daṭṭhabbaṃ atthi imasmiṃ kāye kesātiādīsu  viya ti padassa atthaṃ dassento ti āha yañhi saṃvijjati taṃ upalabbhatīti aṅganti etehi taṃsamaṅgipuggalā nihīnabhāvaṃ gacchantīti  rāgādayo añjati makkhetīti  malādi añjeti tattha ṭhitaṃ ahundaratāya abhibyañjetīti  vivaṭo bhūmipadeso dosādīnaṃ pavattiākāravisesatāya nānappakārā bahulappavattiyā nti lāmakānaṃ nti akosallasambhūtānaṃ nti icchāvasena pavattānaṃ ti aṅgaṇanti laddhanāmena yathāvuttakilesena saha vattati
 tādisassa yonisomanasikārassa abhāvā yesaṃ kilesānaṃ atthitā tesaṃ sappaṭibhayatā visesato jānitabbāti dassetuṃ tiādi vuttaṃ tattha ti pharusā ti kururā ti na uppādetabbā ti yathābhūtasabhāvato ti ime kilesā nāmātiādinā vuttappakārena ti navakammesu vā pariyattidhutaṅgādīsu vā yena vā tena vā ti niddhāraṇe bhummaṃ taṃ pana niddhāraṇaṃ saṅgaṇānaṅgaṇasamudāyatoti dassento ti vatvā puna tadekadesato dassento ti āha tañhi dvayaṃ paṭhamaṃ hīnaseṭṭhabhāvena niddhārīyati paṭhamaṃ uddiṭṭhattā niddhāraṇañhi kvaci kutoci kenaci hotīti
 kiñcāpi aññattha janako hetu pariggāhato paccayo asādhāraṇo hetu sādhāraṇo paccayo sabhāgo hetu asabhāgo paccayo pubbakāliko hetu sahappavatto paccayotiādinā  hetupaccayā vibhajja vuccanti idha pana cattāro kho bhikkhave mahābhūtā hetū cattāro mahābhūtā paccayā rūpakkhandhassa paññāpanāyātiādīsu  viya hetupaccayasaddā samānatthāti dassetuṃ ti vuttaṃ tattha ti hetupaccayavacanadvayena  āyasmā mahāmoggallāno desanaṃ vaḍḍhetukāmo ti anujānanasambhāvanatthe nipāto kiṃ anujānāti samānepi dvinnaṃ sāṅgaṇabhāve tassā pajānanāppajānanahetukataṃ tesaṃ seṭṭhahīnataṃ kiṃ sambhāveti therassa vicittapaṭibhānatāya nānāhetūpamāhi alaṅkatvā yathāpucchitassa atthassa pākaṭakaraṇaṃ tenāha tiādi  seṭṭhahīnabhāve tathāakkhātabbatāpi hi tesaṃ tannimittā evāti
nti tesaṃ dvinnaṃ puggalānaṃ hīnaseṭṭhatāya kāraṇaṃ opammehi nti sutte anantaraṃ vuccamānaṃ vīriyārambhābhāvena aṅgaṇassa appahānaṃ tenāha ti nti kattukamyatāsaṅkhātaṃ aṅgaṇassa pahātukamyatāvasena uppajjanakakusaladhammacchandaṃ ti na uppādessati kusalo vāyāmo nāma chandato balavāti āha ti chandampi anuppādento kathaṃ tajjaṃ vāyāmaṃ karissatīti adhippāyo  ussoḷhībhāvappattaṃ daḷhaṃ vīriyaṃ sāṅgaṇaggahaṇeneva aṅgaṇānaṃ kilesavatthutāya cittassa saṃkiliṭṭhatāya saddhāya puna saṃkiliṭṭhaggahaṇaṃ savisesaṃ kiliṭṭhabhāvavibhāvananti āha ti tiādīsupi tehiyevāti ānetvā sambandhitabbaṃ ukkhalipucchanacoḷakassa viya vasāpītapilotikā viya ca dummocanīyabhāvena malaggahaṇaṃ  pīḷanaṃ hiṃsanaṃ avipphārikatākaraṇaṃ  darathapariḷāhuppādanena paridahanaṃ upatāpanaṃ nti kālanaṃ yathāgahitassa attabhāvassa khepanaṃ āyukkhayanti attho ti pavattessati pāpuṇissatīti vuttaṃ hoti tathābhūto ca pāṇaṃ cajissati nāmāti āha ti
ti upamānidassane nipāto tadatthaṃ dassento ti āha ti -saddena jallādīnaṃ saṅgaho ti -saddena chārikāparimajjanādīnaṃ saṅgahoti abhirūpāya kaññā dātabbātiādīsu viya antarenapi atisayatthabodhakasaddena atisayattho ñāyatīti āha ti nti anumatipucchāviseso ti aparibhoga-apariyodapanarajopathanikkhipanehi kiliṭṭhabhāvaṃ āpādiyamānā ti yathūpanītaṃ upamaṃ upameyyatthena  samaṃ katvā paṭipādento saṃsandentoti attho ti sāṅgaṇo tasmiṃ attabhāve asujjhanakapuggalo āpaṇādito kulagharaṃ ānītassa malaggahitakaṃsabhājanassa tattha laddhabbāya visuddhiyā alābhato yathā anukkamena saṃkiliṭṭhatarabhāvo evaṃ gharato nikkhantassa puggalassa pabbajjāya laddhabbāya visuddhiyā alābhato anukkamena saṃkiliṭṭhatarabhāvoti dassento tiādimāha saṃkiliṭṭhatarabhāvo ca nāma pabbajitassa ājīvavipattivasena vā siyā ācāradiṭṭhisīlavipattīsu aññataravasena vāti taṃ sabbaṃ saṅgahetvā dassetuṃ tiādi vuttaṃ pācittiyavītikkamanaggahaṇena hi ekaccadiṭṭhivipattiyāpi saṅgaho hotīti ti etissaṃ ājīvavipattiyaṃ ṭhitassa iminā nayena sesesupi yathārahaṃ vattabbaṃ sabbaparisasādhāraṇā mahātherassa desanā tasmā gahapativasenapi yojetabbaṃ tattha ukkaṃsagatasaṃkiliṭṭhatarabhāvaṃ dassento nti āha ti yathā attano sīle vā diṭṭhiyā vā visuddhi hoti evaṃ kilesamalinacittasantānaṃ avisodhetvā
ti upanissayādisampattiyā tasmiṃ attabhāve visuddhapuggalo ti iminā dhovanaghaṃsanādīhi pariyodapanaṃ ādimantaṃ katvā vadati  yattha vā na rajena okirīyati ti ettakā udakā vālukā vā ānetabbāti daṇḍakammaṃ katvā ti parisuddhe sīle ṭhitassa sammāvattapaṭipattisīlehi sīlavisuddhi dassitā vattapaṭipattiyāpi hi aṅgaṇānaṃ vikkhambhanaṃ siyā tathā hissā saṃkiliṭṭhakaṃsapātiyā parisuddhapariyodātabhāvo upamābhāvena vutto  kilesavikkhambhanaṃ kilesānaṃ tadaṅganivāraṇaṃ ti sattasupi ṭhānesu parisuddhapariyodātabhāvo viyāti padaṃ ānetvā sambandhitabbaṃ pabbajitassa hi visuddhi nāma heṭṭhimantena sīlavisuddhiyā vā siyā kammaṭṭhānānuyogavasena vivekavāsena jhānassādhigamena vā vipassanābhāvanāya vā sāmaññaphalādhigamena vāti
nti  rāguppattihetubhūtaṃ visabhāgārammaṇaṃ sandhāya vadati nti nti iṭṭhārammaṇe ti muṭṭhassati nti subhanimittaṃ ti ayoniso āvajjissati  aññena avomisso kusalavārapacchindanameva cettha  daṭṭhabbaṃ nti sāṅgaṇo saṃkiliṭṭhacittotiādi ti paṭhamavāre vuttanayānusārena nti mātughātādiānantariyakaraṇapariyosānaṃ sabbaṃ upamāsaṃsandanavacanaṃ
ti  satisammosābhāvato upaṭṭhitassati bhāvatoti attho nti so arāgotiādi dhovanaghaṃsanasaṇhachārikāparimajjanādīhītiādinā  ko nu khotiādi pucchāvasena āgataṃ idaṃ nigamanavasenāti ayameva viseso
nti tattha tattha nāmato eva vibhāvitaṃ na pana sabhāvato pabhedato vāti sabhāvādito vibhāvanaṃ sandhāyāha ti nti icchāvasena avacaraṇānaṃ nti cittasantānaṃ anupaviṭṭhānaṃ te pana tattha paccayavasena nibbattattā pavattā nāma hontīti āha nti visayabhedena pavattiākārabhedena ca nānāvidhānaṃ kāraṇena na kevalaṃ lābhatthikatā eva atha kho puññavantatā sakkatagarukatā ca ettha kāraṇabhāvena gahetabbāti dassento tiādimāha tena lābhatthikopi na yo koci evaṃ cittaṃ uppādeti puññavā sambhāvanīyoti dasseti  avajjapaṭicchādanabhayena  tathā majjhimā  navakā pana attano navakabhāvena  passatha tumhākaṃ therassa kammanti vighāsādādayo nāma īdisassa santike ovādatthaṃ tumhe āgatāti  nti na ca vata maṃ bhikkhū jāneyyuṃ aho vata maṃ bhikkhū na jāneyyunti yojanā nti ettha -saddo avadhāraṇattho -saddo vacanālaṅkāroti āha ti  icchuppādavāravaṇṇanāya -saddo idha āsannakāraṇatthoti taṃ dassento ti āha   kopaappaccayānameva gahaṇaṃ nti kopaappaccayādhibhūtānanti adhippāyo
ti anurūpe rahasi evameva hi atthaṃ dassetuṃ tiādi vuttaṃ ti lābhatthiko hītiādinā vuttena purimena yojanānayena sadisameva
codanāya paṭipuggalabhāvo codanā ca āpattiyāti cuditakena codakassa samānabhāvo āpattiāpannatāyāti āha ti sappaṭipuggalenevassa codanicchāya kāraṇaṃ vibhāvetuṃ ntiādi vuttaṃ na cāyaṃ sāpattikatāya eva samānataṃ icchati atha kho aññathāpīti dassento tiādimāha aññena vā paṭipuggalena  ayañhi sappaṭipuggalova maṃ codeyyāti icchati evāhaṃ tassa paṭipuggalehi saddhiṃ ekajjhāsayo hutvā tassa upari kiñci vattuṃ kātuṃ vā labhissāmīti  imasmiṃ pana pakkhe ti natthi etassa paṭipuggaloti ti evamattho veditabbo
aho vatāti idaṃ padaṃ dissatīti sambandho imassa puggalassa icchācāre ṭhitattā bhikkhūnaṃ dhammaṃ deseyyāti vacanato ti vuttaṃ na hesa saccaṃ kira tvaṃ bhikkhūtiādinā kiñci vītikkamaṃ uddissa bhagavatā pucchitabbataṃ icchati ti maggabhāvanaṃ vā phalasacchikiriyaṃ vā sikhāppattavipassanānuyogaṃ vā nirodhasamāpajjanaṃ vā jhānasamāpajjanameva vā antaraṃ kāraṇaṃ katvā bhagavatā attānaṃ paṭipucchitabbaṃ no icchati ntiādinā anumatiggahaṇavasena pucchitabbaṃ icchati uttānameva katvā pucchitabbaṃ icchatīti attho upaharante passatīti sambandho abhabbaṭṭhānabhikkhutāya  sāsanato
nti parivārasampattiñceva bhikkhūhi kariyamānaṃ sakkāragarukārasampattiñca  mayā saṃvibhāge kariyamāne ti sayameva gantvā bhikkhūnaṃ purato attānaṃ dasseti purato vasantaṃ pana bhikkhu purakkhatvā gacchantiyevāti adhippāyo
nti  aggato upanīyamānaṃ dakkhiṇodakaṃ yato eva-kāro tato aññattha niyamo icchito avadhāraṇatthaṃ vā eva-kāraggahaṇanti katvā nti ahaṃ labheyyamevāti evametaṃ avadhāraṇaṃ daṭṭhabbanti adhippāyenāha ti aññathā yathārutavasena avadhāraṇe gayhamāne na aññe labheyyunti ayamevettha attho siyāti ti idaṃ tassa aggāsanādipaccāsīsanāya kāraṇadassanaṃ
nti maṅgalāmaṅgalesu anumodanāvasena pavattetabbadhammakathaṃ nti anumodanekadesaṃ pubbe anumoditapubbo anumodatūti avatvā 
ti tādisesu pesalānaṃ bahussutānaṃ vasanaṭṭhānesu sabbampi ratiṃ pavattanato  nti anekavihitesu kaṅkhaṭṭhāniyesu kaṅkhāvinayanāya taṃ taṃ pañhānaṃ vinicchaye kusalānaṃ chekānaṃ tesu tesu dhammakathikesu ajjhiṭṭhesu vārena dhammaṃ kathentesu ayaṃ byattoti dhammajjhesakena ajjhiṭṭhattā 
nti bhikkhū yaṃ mama abhivādanapaccuṭṭhānañjalikammasāmīcikammādiṃ karonti taṃ ādareneva kareyyuṃ yañca me parikkhārajātaṃ paṭiyādenti tampi sundaraṃ sammadeva abhisaṅkhataṃ kareyyunti attho nti pāsāṇacchattaṃ viya garukātabbaṃ nti etaṃ sakkareyyuntiādinā vuttasakkārādividhiṃ ti tena kāraṇena bāhusaccādiguṇavisesavato eva sakkārādīnaṃ arahattāti attho  īdisaṃ piyo garūtiādinā  vuttappakāraṃ nti evaṃ sakkareyyuntiādinā vuttappakāraṃ sakkārādiṃ kareyyuṃ ti yoyaṃ bhikkhuvāre vuttavidhi eseva nayo  bhikkhunīvārādīsu 
nti etthāpi heṭṭhā vuttanayeneva avadhāraṇaṃ gahetabbaṃ piṇḍapātassa paṇītatā upasecanādivasenāti āha nti  nti nidassanamattaṃ utusappāyānaṃ nivātānaṃ phassitatalānaṃ pihitadvārakavāḷavātapānādīnampi paṇītasenāsanabhāvato -saddena vā tesampi gahaṇaṃ daṭṭhabbaṃ ti sabbesu tesu catūsupi paccayavāresu
ti idaṃ na kāyakammaṃ cakkhuviññeyyaṃ kāyakammunā pana saha pavattaṃ oṭṭhaparipphandanaṃ bhākuṭikaraṇaṃ kāyaṅgādidassanaṃ kāyakammadassanaṃ viya hotīti katvā vuttaṃ ti etthāpi eseva nayo tasmā kāyavikārajanakā dhammā dissantīti vuttā vacīvikārajanakā sūyantīti tato eva ca te  sammukhakāle  nāma  asammukhakāle  nāma anurūpato gahaṇaṃ  nti tassa bhikkhuno dhutaguṇattānurūpato gaṇhāti tenāha ti araññe nivāso assāti  pantaṃ pariyantaṃ dūrataraṃ senāsanaṃ assāti  taṃ pana atthamattena dassentena ti vuttaṃ bhikkhāsaṅkhātānaṃ piṇḍānaṃ pāto piṇḍāpāto taṃ piṇḍapātaṃ uñchati gavesatīti  piṇḍāya patituṃ carituṃ vatametassāti vā piṇḍapāti so eva  dānato avakhaṇḍanato apetaṃ apadānaṃ saha apadānena sapadānaṃ anavakhaṇḍanaṃ anugharaṃ caraṇasīlo  unnatabhāvena paṃsukūlaṃ viya paṃsukūlaṃ paṃsu viya vā kucchitabhāvaṃ ulati gacchatīti paṃsukūlaṃ tassa dhāraṇaṃ idha paṃsukūlaṃ taṃ sīlamassāti 
 agghaphassavaṇṇaparihānito apaṃsukūlampi ko pana vādo paṃsukūlanti adhippāyo ti thūlena olambamānena dīghasuttakena ti ettha phassenapi parihāyatīti vattabbaṃ tañhi tattha kharaphassampi hotiyevāti kasmā pana pāḷiyaṃ āraññikādiggahaṇena cattārova dhutaguṇā vuttāti padhānattā taggahaṇeneva ca ito paresampi sukhaparibhogatāya gahaṇasambhavato yo hi āraññiko pantasenāsano tassa abbhokāsika-rukkhamūlika-nesajjika-yathāsanthatika-sosānikaṅgāni suparipūrāni yo ca piṇḍapātiko sapadānacārī ca tassa pattapiṇḍikakhalupacchābhattikaekāsanikaṅgāni yo pana paṃsukūliko tassa  tecīvarikaṅgaṃ supariharamevāti padhānattā hi bhagavatāpi kadāhaṃ nandaṃ passeyyaṃ āraññaṃ paṃsukūlikantiādinā  tattha tattha āraññikādayo eva gayhanti ti pāḷiyaṃ āgatānaṃ paricchijja gahaṇametaṃ na ettakā sabbepi ekassa ekaṃsato sambhavanti nāpi ettakāyeva pāpadhammā pahātabbā na hi makkhapaḷāsādīnaṃ appahīnabhāvepi ti
nti yassa kassacītiādinā vuttamatthaṃ ti anvayato byatirekato ca udāharaṇena vibhāvento  ativiya duggandhatāya sā ca ahīnaṃ tikhiṇakopatāya kukkuramanussānaṃ odanakummāsūpacayatāya sarīrassa hotīti vadanti nti ahiādīnaṃ ti uparūpari khipanena racitaṃ katvā taṃ pana vaḍḍhitaṃ tena ca bhājanaṃ pūritaṃ hotīti āha ti janassa dassanayogyaṃ dassanīyaṃ  taṃ paramaparisuddhaṃ manoharañca hotīti āha nti abhinavaniviṭṭhā mahāmātā  sā pana puttalābhayogyataṃ upādāya maṅgalavacanena janīti vuccati tassā niyyamānaṃ paṇṇākāraṃ janiyā haratīti  ti atthadvaye nti āmeḍitavacanamāha na manāpaṃ etassāti amanāpo tassa bhāvo  tathāpavatto cittuppādoti āha nti buddhavesattā liṅgassa   icchāvacarehi santānassa bharitabhāvo so pana tesaṃ appahīnatāyāti āha nti
 tena gāmantavihāraṃ anuggaṇhātīti vattabbe nti pana potthake likhitaṃ na hi sukkapakkhe pāḷiyaṃ āraññikaggahaṇaṃ atthi sati ca icchāvacarappahāne gāmantavihāro ekantena na paṭikkhipitabbo icchitabbova tādisānaṃ uttarimanussadhammapaṭicchādanato  tathā hi vakkhati tiādi  manuññabhāvato tittihetuto ca
nti ca upayogavacanaṃ paṭi-saddayogena attho pana sampadānamevāti āha nti ca ti  samayanti  gijjhakūṭapaṇḍavaisigilivebhāravepullapabbatānaṃ vasena  ti samīpatthe bhummavacananti āha ti
ti purāṇe pabbajitato pubbe yānakāraputto tathāpaññāto nti gomuttakuṭilaṃ tenāha nti ti paṇḍuputto ti samiti ti cintitacintitaṭṭhānameva tacchati tañca kho na tassa cittānusārena atha kho attano suttānusārena tacchanto yānakāraputto nti attano cittena mama cittaṃ jānitvā viya
na saddhāya pabbajitoti imināva kammaphalasaddhāya abhāvo nesaṃ pakāsitoti āha ti pabbajitānaṃ jīvikā attho etesanti  tenāha tiādi  vuccati sāṭheyyaṃ saṭhānaṃ guṇavāṇijakānaṃ kammaṃ sāṭheyyanti āha tiādi tucchasabhāvena māno naḷo viyāti naḷo mānasaṅkhāto uggato naḷo etesanti  tenāha ti lahukatāya vā  pharusavacanatāya  tiracchānakathābahulatāya  ti idaṃ kammadvārādīnaṃ asaṃvutabhāvo uppattidvārānaṃ asaṃvutatāya eva hotīti katvā vuttaṃ atha vā ti nimitte bhummaṃ chasu indriyesu nimittabhūtesu asaṃvutakammadvārāti attho ti bhojane ayuttapariyesana-ayuttapaṭiggahaṇa-ayuttaparibhoge vajjetvā yuttapariyesana-yuttapaṭiggahaṇa-yuttaparibhogasaṅkhātā yā mattā appamattehi  tenāha ti ti rattindivaṃ āvaraṇiyehi dhammehi cittaparisodhanasaṅkhāte jāgare tesaṃ jāgaritāya adhisīlasikkhāya gāravarahitānaṃ itarasikkhāsu patiṭṭhā eva natthīti dassento ti vatvā tameva gāravābhāvaṃ sarūpena vibhāvento ti āha
pakatiyāpi  siddhāya ratanattayasaddhāya kammaphalasaddhāya ca   yathā taṃ dravabhūtaṃ amataṃ laddhā  yathā taṃ bahalapiṇḍikasudhābhojanaṃ laddhā  sādhu sādhūti tameva pana sādhukāraṃ hadaye ṭhapetvā  ettha ca attamanavācānicchāraṇaṃ pivanasadisaṃ katvā vuttaṃ bahiddhābhāvato manasā abbhanumodanaṃ pana abbhantarabhāvato ghasanasadisaṃ vuttaṃ saṅkhādanajjhoharaṇañhi ghasananti rassañca ekavacanaṃ hotīti āha ti dīghañca bahuvacanaṃ hotīti āha nti upari hotīti ānetvā sambandho ti ālasiyena vā ñātibyasanādīhi vā ti vatvā tattha kāraṇaṃ vibhāvento tiādimāha tattha na gacchantīti nāgā na āgacchantīti nāgā na āguṃ karontīti nāgāti yo vividho vacanattho icchito taṃ vicāretvā dassetuṃ tiādi vuttaṃ taṃ pana ñeyyāvabodhāya vacanato appamattakāraṇaṃ
sayameva  sabbathā maggena pahīnaāguttā so kāmayogādike  dasavidhasaṃyojanappabhedāni ca sabbabandhanāni  jahitvā  yakkhādīsu sabbesu vā bhavesu kenaci saṅgena  tīhi ca vimuttīhi  tato eva iṭṭhādīsu tādibhāvappattiyā  so vuttalakkhaṇena  taṃsabhāvattā ti attho veditabbo tenāha ti  aggasāvakattā guṇavisesayogato nti aññamaññassa subhāsitato sampaṭicchanena samappavattamodatāya samaṃ sadisaṃ abbhanumodiṃsu taṃ pana samanumodanaṃ tiādinā pāḷivaseneva dasseti



nti  paripuṇṇaṃ samantato pannaṃ pattanti sampannaṃ tenāha ti nti suvāti vuttaṃ suvagaṇaṃ ti sammadeva panno gato upagato tenāha ti nti sampattiyuttaṃ sā panettha rasasampatti adhippetā sāmaññajotanāya visese avaṭṭhānato tenāha nti niddosanti attho tena vuttaṃ ti sīlassa anavasesasamādānena akhaṇḍādibhāvāpattiyā ca  samādānato paṭṭhāya acchindanato  samādānato hi accantavirodhidhammānuppattiyā sīlasamaṅgitā veditabbā cetanādīnaṃ pana sīlanalakkhaṇānaṃ dhammānaṃ pavattikkhaṇe vattabbameva natthi    tasmā tattha vuttanayeneva vitthārakathā veditabbāti adhippāyo
ti nissitapāripūriyā nissayapāripūrimāha nissitakammavipattisampattivisayattā yathā mañcā ukkuṭṭhiṃ karontīti tathā hi khettena khaṇḍapūtiādidoso vutto ti aparipūraṃ hoti sassapāripūriyā abhāvato tenevāha ti pādamattassapi anekambaṇaphalanato  kisalayapalālādibahutāya  nti yathā khittaṃ bījaṃ khaṇḍādicatudosavasena aparipuṇṇaṃ hoti tadabhāvena ca paripuṇṇaṃ evaṃ sīlaṃ khaṇḍādicatudosavasena aparipuṇṇaṃ hoti tadabhāvena ca paripuṇṇanti catudosatadabhāvasāmaññameva nidassananidassitabbavipattisampattīsu dasseti  vipākaphalena nti vipulānisaṃsaṃ svāyaṃ ānisaṃso idha pāḷiyaṃ nānappakārena vitthārīyati
ti  -saddo arucisūcanattho tenettha ācariyavādassa attano aruccanabhāvaṃ dīpeti ti anāmaṭṭhavisesaṃ sāmaññato sīlasaṅkhepena gahitaṃ tañca catubbidhanti ācariyatthero ti āha ti catupārisuddhisīle nti  padhānasīlaṃ ti uddesaniddese idha  niddese viya uddesepi  sampannasīlāti vuttattāti adhippāyo  sīlaggahaṇañhi pāḷiyaṃ pātimokkhasaṃvaravasena āgataṃ tenāha tiādi tattha avadhāraṇena itaresaṃ tiṇṇaṃ ekadesena pātimokkhantogadhabhāvaṃ dīpeti tathā hi anolokiyolokane ājīvahetu chasikkhāpadavītikkame gilānapaccayassa apaccavekkhitaparibhoge ca āpatti vihitāti ti indriyasaṃvarasīlādīni ti sīlapariyāyena tesaṃ katthaci sutte gahitaṭṭhānaṃ nāma kiṃ atthi yathā pātimokkhasaṃvaroti ācariyassa sammukhattā apaṭikkhipantova upacārena pucchanto viya vadati tenāha ti ti tassa sallahukabhāvamāha cittādhiṭṭhānamattena paṭipākatikabhāvāpattito itaradvayepi eseva nayo nti phalena hetuṃ dasseti uppādanahetukā hi paccayānaṃ uppatti nti idaṃ payojanaṃ imassa paccayassa paribhuñjaneti adhippāyo ti iminā indriyasaṃvarādīni tīṇi padhānassa sīlassa parivāravasena pavattiyā pariyāyasīlāni nāmāti dasseti
idāni pātimokkhasaṃvarasseva padhānabhāvaṃ byatirekato anvayato ca upamāya vibhāvetuṃ tiādimāha tattha ti pātimokkhasaṃvaro ti indriyasaṃvarādīni ti sampannasīlāti ettha yaṃ sīlaṃ vuttaṃ tasseva ti ettha pātimokkhaggahaṇena  yathā aññathāpi idha bhikkhu sīlavā hotīti  puggalādhiṭṭhānāya desanāya uddiṭṭhaṃ sīlaṃ pātimokkhasaṃvarasaṃvuto viharatīti  niddiṭṭhaṃ
ti yo naṃ pāti rakkhati taṃ mokkheti moceti āpāyikādīhi dukkhehīti pātimokkhanti laddhanāmena sikkhāpadasīlena pihitakāyavacīdvārā te pana yasmā evaṃbhūtā tena samannāgatā nāma honti tasmā vuttaṃ ti
aparo  nayo   kilesānaṃ balavabhāvato pāpakiriyāya sukarabhāvato puññakiriyāya ca dukkarabhāvato bahukkhattuṃ apāyesu patanasīloti pātī puthujjano aniccatāya vā bhavādīsu kammavegakkhitto ghaṭīyantaṃ viya anavaṭṭhānena paribbhamanato gamanasīloti pātī maraṇavasena vā tamhi tamhi sattanikāye attabhāvassa pātanasīloti pātī sattasantāno cittameva vā taṃ pātiṃ saṃsāradukkhato mokkhetīti  cittassa hi vimokkhena satto vimuttoti vuccati vuttañhi cittavodānā visujjhantīti anupādāya āsavehi cittaṃ vimuttanti  ca
atha vā avijjādinā hetunā saṃsāre patati gacchati pavattatīti pātī avijjānīvaraṇānaṃ sattānaṃ taṇhāsaṃyojanānaṃ sandhāvataṃ saṃsaratanti  hi vuttaṃ tassa pātino sattassa taṇhādisaṃkilesattayato mokkho etenāti  kaṇṭhekālotiādīnaṃ viya samāsasiddhi veditabbā
atha vā pāteti vinipāteti dukkheti pāti cittaṃ vuttañhi cittena nīyati loko cittena parikassatīti  tassa pātino mokkho etenāti  patati vā etena apāyadukkhe saṃsāradukkhe cāti pātī taṇhādisaṃkileso vuttañhi taṇhā janeti purisaṃ  taṇhādutiyo purisoti  ca ādi tato pātito mokkhoti 
atha vā patati etthāti pātī cha ajjhattikabāhirāni āyatanāni vuttañhi chasu loko samuppanno chasu kubbati santhavanti  tato ajjhattikabāhirāyatanasaṅkhātato pātito mokkhoti  atha vā pāto vinipāto assa atthīti pātī saṃsāro tato mokkhoti  atha vā sabbalokādhipatibhāvato dhammissaro bhagavā patīti vuccati muccati etenāti mokkho patino mokkho tena paññattattāti pātimokkho  pātimokkho eva  sabbaguṇānaṃ vā mūlabhāvato uttamaṭṭhena pati ca so yathāvuttatthena mokkho cāti pātimokkho pātimokkho eva  tathā hi vuttaṃ pātimokkhantiādimetaṃ mukhametaṃ pamukhametanti  vitthāro
atha vā -iti pakāre ti accantatthe nipāto tasmā pakārehi accantaṃ mokkhetīti  idañhi sīlaṃ sayaṃ tadaṅgavasena samādhisahitaṃ paññāsahitañca vikkhambhanavasena samucchedavasena ca accantaṃ mokkheti mocetīti  pati pati mokkhoti vā pātimokkho tamhā tamhā vītikkamadosato paccekaṃ mokkhoti attho pātimokkho eva  mokkho vā nibbānaṃ tassa mokkhassa patibimbabhūtoti pātimokkho  sīlasaṃvaro hi nibbedhabhāgiyo sūriyassa aruṇuggamanaṃ viya nibbānassa udayabhūto tappaṭibhāgo viya hoti yathārahaṃ kilesanibbāpanatoti pātimokkho pātimokkhoyeva  atha vā mokkhaṃ pati vattati mokkhābhimukhanti vā pātimokkhaṃ pātimokkhameva nti evamettha pātimokkhasaddassa attho veditabbo
ti kāyikavācasikaavītikkamasaṅkhātena ācārena ceva navesiyagocaratādisaṅkhātena gocarena ca sampannā sampannaācāragocarāti attho ti atiparittakesu anāpattigamanīyesu dukkaṭadubbhāsitamattesūti apare ti gārayhesu te pana ekantato akusalasabhāvā hontīti āha ti ti bhayato dassanasīlā paramāṇumattampi vajjaṃ sineruppamāṇaṃ viya katvā bhāyanasīlā ti sammadeva sakkaccaṃ sabbaso ca ādiyitvā ti niddhāraṇe bhummanti samudāyato avayavaniddhāraṇaṃ dassento ti atthamāha sikkhāpadameva hi samādātabbaṃ sikkhitabbañcāti adhippāyo ti sikkhākoṭṭhāsesu mūlapaññattianupaññatisabbatthapaññattipadesapaññattiādibhedaṃ yaṃ kiñci sikkhitabbaṃ paṭipajjitabbaṃ pūretabbaṃ sīlaṃ taṃ pana dvāravasena duvidhamevāti āha ti imasmiṃ atthavikappe ti ādhāre bhummaṃ sikkhābhāgesu kassaci visuṃ aggahaṇato tenāha nti
nti  desanāya kāraṇapucchā nti payojananiddeso ko attho kva attho kva nipātitāti nayidamevaṃ daṭṭhabbaṃ nti hi ettha byatirekato yaṃ sīlānisaṃsassa adassanaṃ taṃ imissā desanāya kāraṇanti kasmā āraddhanti vineyyānaṃ sīlānisaṃsassa adassanatoti atthato āpanno eva hotīti tenāha tiādi nti pana imassa atthaṃ vivarituṃ ntiādi vuttaṃ ti udayo sīlavā sīlasampanno kāyassa bhedā paraṃ maraṇā sugatiṃ saggalokaṃ upapajjatītiādīsu  pana vipākaphalampi ānisaṃsoti vuttaṃ ti ko phalaviseso ti ko abbhudayo vijjamānopi guṇo yāthāvato vibhāvito eva abhiruciṃ uppādeti na avibhāvito tasmā ekantato ānisaṃsakittanaṃ icchitabbamevāti dassetuṃ  udāhaṭo
tattha  nāma ucchurasaṃ pacitvā cuṇṇādīhi missitvā sampiṇḍane piṇḍībhūtaṃ  apiṇḍitaṃ dravībhūtaṃ  bhijjanakkhamaṃ  nāma phalikasadisā ti -saddena macchaṇḍikānaṃ saṅgaho tasmiṃ kāle guḷādīsu visakaṇṭakavohāro apaccantadese pacuroti ti vuttaṃ  visakaṇṭakaṃ mā gaṇhantūti
ti piyāyitabbo piyassa nāma dassanaṃ ekantato abhinanditabbaṃ hotīti āha ti pītisamuṭṭhānapasannasommarūpapariggahañhi cakkhu piyacakkhūti vuccati nti sabrahmacārīnaṃ ti pītimanassa paribrūhanato uparūpari pīticittassa uppādako ti garukaraṇassa ṭhānabhūto ti ñāṇena jānitabbaṃ jānāti yathā vā aññe ajānantāpi jānantā viya pavattanti na evamayaṃ ayaṃ pana jānanto eva jānāti  ti dassanabhūtena paññācakkhunā passitabbaṃ passati passanto eva vā passati ti evaṃ viññutāya paṇḍitabhāvena sambhāvetabbo
ti sīlesu paripūrakārī eva bhaveyyāti evaṃ uttarapadāvadhāraṇaṃ daṭṭhabbaṃ evañhi iminā padena uparisikkhādvayaṃ anivattitameva hoti yathā pana sīlesu paripūrakārī nāma hoti taṃ phalena dassetuṃ ntiādi vuttaṃ vipassanādhiṭṭhānasamādhisaṃvattanikatāya hi idha sīlassa pāripūrī na kevalaṃ akhaṇḍādibhāvamattaṃ tenāha yāni kho pana tāni akhaṇḍāni samādhisaṃvattanikānīti evañca katvā upari sikkhādvayaṃ sīlassa sambhārabhāvena gahitanti sīlassevettha padhānaggahaṇaṃ siddhaṃ hoti tathā hi cittekaggatāsaṅkhārapariggahānaṃ sīlassānurakkhaṇabhāvaṃ vakkhati yaṃ pana vakkhati sikkhattayadesanā jātāti  taṃ itarāsampi sikkhānaṃ idha gahitatāmattaṃ sandhāya vuttaṃ na padhānabhāvena gahitataṃ yadi evaṃ kathaṃ sīlassa appamattakatāvacanaṃ vuttañhetaṃ appamattakaṃ kho panetaṃ bhikkhave oramattakanti  taṃ puthujjanagocaraṃ sandhāya vuttaṃ tathā hi tattha na nippadesato sīlaṃ vibhattaṃ evaṃ katvā tattha sīlamattakanti mattaggahaṇaṃ samatthitanti daṭṭhabbaṃ ti akhaṇḍādibhāvena kassaci vā ahāpanena upapannena ti karaṇena sampādanena ti cittasamādhāne ti aviyutto pasuto yo sabbena sabbaṃ jhānabhāvanaṃ ananuyutto so taṃ bahi nīharati nāma yo ārabhitvā antarā saṅkocaṃ āpajjati  so taṃ vināseti nāma yo pana īdiso ahutvā jhānaṃ upasampajja viharati so ti dassento tiādimāha
aniccassa tebhūmakadhammassa aniccanti vā anupassanā  tathā  ca tasseva nibbindanākārena pavattā anupassanā  virajjanākārena pavattā anupassanā  nirodhassa anupassanā  paṭinissajjanavasena pavattā anupassanā  suññāgāragato bhikkhu tattha laddhakāyavivekatāya samathavipassanāvasena cittavivekaṃ  paribrūhento yathānusiṭṭhaṃ paṭipattiyā lokaṃ sāsanañca attano visesādhigamaṭṭhānabhūtaṃ suññāgārañca upasobhayamāno guṇavisesādhiṭṭhānabhāvāpādanena viññūnaṃ atthato taṃ brūhento nāma hotīti vuttaṃ nti tenāha tiādi ayameva suññāgārānubrūhanaviññuppasatthānaṃ bhājanaṃ na senāsanapatiṭṭhāpananti dassento āha ti ggahaṇena cettha araññarukkhamūlādi sabbaṃ padhānānuyogakkhamaṃ senāsanaṃ gahitanti daṭṭhabbaṃ
ti ajjhattikassa upādāyāti  ādinayappavattaṃ taṇhāvicaritasuttaṃ ti taṇhāsannissayattā na hi taṇhāvirahitā mānadiṭṭhipavatti atthi ti dassetabbatāya mānadiṭṭhiyo ogāhetvāti attho gahaṇatthameva hi desetabbadhammassa desanāya osaraṇaṃ  sattasantānassa saṃsāre papañcanato anuppabandhanavasena vitthāraṇato ti sīlādhiṭṭhānattā
adhicittasikkhā vuttāti ānetvā sambandho vipassanāvasena suññāgāravaḍḍhaneti yojanā ti adhicittādhipaññāsikkhā ti adhisīlasikkhāya saddhiṃ saṅgahetvā vuttā yadi evamayaṃ sikkhattayadesanā jātāti sikkhattayānisaṃsappakāsanī siyāti anuyogaṃ sandhāyāha tiādi tattha yaṃ vattabbaṃ taṃ heṭṭhā vuttameva indriyasaṃvaro viya pātimokkhasaṃvarassa catupārisuddhisīlassa ārakkhabhūtā cittekaggatā vipassanā ca idha gahitāti tadubhayaṃ appadhānaṃ sīlameva pana padhānabhāvena gahitanti veditabbaṃ tenāha tiādi
nti  samuppannabyādhidukkhato balavataraṃ taṃ abhibhavituṃ samatthaṃ jhānasukhaṃ uppajjati  tena daḷhaattasinehena viluttahadayo kusaladhamme chaḍḍento  suddho saṅkhārapuñjoti yāthāvadassanena  ahaṃkāramamaṃkārābhāvato dubbhikkhabhaye khudābhibhavaṃ sandhāyāha ti byādhibhayaṃ sandhāyāha ussussati visussanīti ādi-saddena gahitaṃ corabhayaṃ sandhāyāha ti ti samathavipassanādvayassa ettha ca ajjhattaṃ ceto suññāgārānanti imehi visesanibbedhabhāgiyabhāvāpādanena sīlaṃ rakkhituṃ samatthā eva cittekaggatāvipassanā gahitā yasmā parato jhānavimokkhaphalābhiññāṇaadhiṭṭhānabhāvo sīlassa uddhaṭo tasmā tassa bhiyyopi sambhārabhūtā eva cittekaggatā vipassanā tattha tattha gahitāti veditabbā
ti -saddena yathāvuttacittekaggatāvipassanā saṅgaṇhāti sīlassa vā mūlakāraṇabhūtaṃ sabbaṃ kammassakatañāṇañca saṅgaṇhāti kammapathasammādiṭṭhiṃ vā sīlañhi tadaññampi puññakiriyāvatthu teneva parisodhitaṃ mahapphalaṃ hoti mahānisaṃsanti nti lābhā sāya saṃvaraṇasīlaparipūraṇaṃ pāḷiyaṃ āgataṃ kimīdisaṃ bhagavā anujānātīti na bhagavā sabhāvena īdisaṃ anujānāti mahākāruṇikatāya pana puggalajjhāsayena evaṃ vuttanti dassento tiādimāha tattha  vācaṃ ti chinnakatho mūgo viya hutvā obhāsaparikathānimittaviññattipayuttaṃ ghāsesanaṃ vācaṃ na bhaṇe na katheyyāti attho ti saṅkhepato vuttamatthaṃ vivaranto tiādimāha raso sabhāvabhūto ānisaṃso 
ti cīvarādipaccayavasena dānakārā ti vuttavacanaṃ pākaṭīkātumāha tiādi pañcime gahapatayo ānisaṃsātiādīsu  anisaṃsasaddo phalapariyāyopi hotīti āha nti
sassusasurā ca tappakkhikā ca  te ñātiyonisambandhena āvāhavivāhasambandhavasena sambandhā  ti yonisambandhavasena ti ekena samānena lohitasambandhena sambaddhā ti petūpapattivasena nibbattiṃ  upagatā te pana yasmā idha katakālakiriyā kālena katajīvitupacchedā honti tasmā vuttaṃ ti ti pasannacittako kālakato  pitā vā mātā vā petayoniṃ upapannoti adhikārato viññāyatīti vuttaṃ ti tassa tathā sīlasampannattāti adhippāyo ariyabhāve pana sati vattabbameva natthi tenāha tiādi nti bahupakāraṃ nti abhivādanādivasena upagamanaṃ nti upaṭṭhānanti
ti madditā ti riñcanā anabhirati ananuyogo sīlavā bhikkhu attano sīlakhaṇḍabhayena samāhito vipassako ca paccayaghātena aratiyā ratiyā ca sahitā abhibhavitāva hotīti āha tiādi
 bhāyatīti   bhāyati etasmāti  purimavārasadisattā ti atidisitvāpi puna taṃ dassetuṃ tiādi vuttaṃ therassa heṭṭhā nisinnattā devatāya  sukhena vattituṃ  asamatthā
adhikaṃ cetoti  upacārajjhānacittaṃ tassa pana adhikatā pākatikakāmāvacaracittehi sundaratāya sapaṭipakkhato visuddhiyā cāti āha nti nti samādhimāha so ca upacārasamādhi daṭṭhabbo vivekajaṃ pītisukhaṃ samādhijaṃ pītisukhaṃ apītijaṃ jhānasukhaṃ satipārisuddhijaṃ jhānasukhanti catubbidhampi jhānasukhaṃ paṭipakkhato nikkhantataṃ upādāya nekkhammasukhanti vuccatīti āha ti  iminā tesu jhānesu samāpajjanavasībhāvamāha nikāmalābhīti pana vacanato āvajjanādhiṭṭhānapaccavekkhaṇavasiyopi vuttā evāti veditabbā ti etena tesaṃ jhānasukhakhippābhiññatañca dasseti nti vepullaṃ pāpitānaṃ jhānānaṃ vipulatā nāma subhāvitabhāvena ciratarappatti sā ca paricchedānurūpāva icchitabbbāti vipulānanti vatvā ti  āha paricchedakālañhi appatvāva vuṭṭhahanto akasiralābhī na hoti yāvadicchakaṃ pavattetuṃ asamatthattā idāni teyeva yathāvutte samāpajjanādivasībhāve byatirekavasena vibhāvetuṃ tiādi vuttaṃ tattha ti idaṃ paṭiladdhamattassa jhānassa vasena vuttaṃ ti icchiticchitakkhaṇe ti vasībhāvassa paccanīkadhamme jhānādhigamassa pana paccanīkadhammā pageva vikkhambhitā aññathā jhānādhigamo eva na siyā ti kicchena visodheti kāmādīnavapaccavekkhaṇādīhi kāmacchandādīnaṃ viya  aññesampi samādhipāribandhikānaṃ dūrasamussāraṇaṃ idha vikkhambhanaṃ visodhanañcāti veditabbaṃ nti kālamānanāḷikāyantaṃ āha
visesena rūpāvacaracatutthajjhānaṃ sabbaso vasībhāvāpāditaṃ abhiññāpādakanti adhippāyenāha ti arūpajjhānampi pana adhiṭṭhānatāya pādakameva cuddasadhā cittaparidamanena vinā tadabhāvato evamabhiññāpādake rūpāvacarajjhāne vutte rūpāvacaratāya kiñcāpi abhiññānaṃ lokiyavāro āgatoti ayañhettha adhippāyo nti abhiññāvāraṃ  sampannasīlasseva lābhato ti gahetvā
ti nīvaraṇādīnaṃ paccanīkadhammānaṃ sudūratarabhāvena jhānaṅgānaṃ vūpasantatāya nibbutasabbadarathapariḷāhatāyāti attho yato tesaṃ jhānānaṃ paṇītatarādibhāvo ti rūpapaṭighādivigamanena saṇhasukhumādibhāvappattasantabhāvena yadaggena hi nesaṃ bhāvanābhisamayasabbhāvitasaṇhasukhumākārāni ārammaṇāni santāni tadaggena jhānaṅgānaṃ santatā veditabbā ārammaṇasantatāya santatā lokuttaradhammārammaṇāhi paccavekkhaṇāhi dīpetabbā vimuttā visesena muttā ye hi jhānadhammā tathāpavattapubbabhāgabhāvanāhi tabbisesatāya sātisayaṃ paṭipakkhadhammehi vimuttivasena pavattanti tato eva tathāvimuttatāya pitu aṅke vissaṭṭhaaṅgapaccaṅgo viya kumāro nirāsaṅkabhāvena ārammaṇe adhimuttā ca pavattanti te vimokkhāti vuccanti tenāha ti  yadipi ārammaṇasamatikkamavasena pattabbāni āruppāni na aṅgātikkamavasena tathāpi yasmā ārammaṇe avirattassa jhānasamatikkamo na hoti samatikkantesu ca jhānesu ārammaṇaṃ samatikkantameva hoti tasmā ārammaṇasamatikkamaṃ avatvā ti icceva vuttaṃ ti pāḷiyaṃ sampādetabbā passitabbāti vā kiñci padaṃ icchitabbaṃ asutaparikappanena pana payojanaṃ natthīti ti vuttaṃ evañca katvā tena virāgabhāvena tesaṃ santatāti ayampi attho vibhāvito hoti rūpajjhānādīnaṃ viya natthi etesaṃ ārammaṇabhūtaṃ vā phalabhūtaṃ vā rūpanti arūpā arūpā eva  tenāha ti ti sahajātanāmasamūhena
ti bandhanti kehīti āha tiādi asamucchinnarāgādikassa  hi khandhādīnaṃ āyatiṃ khandhādīhi sambandho samucchinnarāgādikassa pana taṃ natthi katānampi kammānaṃ asamatthabhāvāpattitoti rāgādīnaṃ anvayato ca saṃyojanaṭṭho siddhoti āha ti ti samucchedena sabbaso āyatiṃ anuppajjanena paṭipakkhadhammānaṃ anavasesato savanato pīḷanato  ariyamaggoti āha nti taṃ sotaṃ ādito panno adhigacchīti  aṭṭhamako tenāha ti paṭhamamaggakkhaṇe puggalassāti adhippāyo idha pana -saddo phalasacchikiriyāya paṭipannotiādīsu  viya vattamānakālikoti āha nti abhītakālikatte pana sarasatova nāmalābho siyā virūpaṃ sadukkhaṃ saupāyāsaṃ nipātetīti  apāyadukkhe khipanako ti sabhāvo tenāha ntiādi ti avinipātadhammatāya kāraṇaṃ pucchati apāyaṃ gamentīti apāyagamanīyā sambujjhatīti  ariyamaggo so pana paṭhamamaggassa adhigatattā avasiṭṭho eva adhigandhabbabhāvena icchitabboti āha nti
na pahātabbānīti adhippāyo oḷārikānaṃ rāgādīnaṃ samucchindanavasena pavattamāno dutiyamaggo avasiṭṭhānaṃ tesaṃ tanubhāvāpattiyā  uppanno nāma hotīti vuttaṃ ti ti kadāci karahaci uppajjanena ti samudācāramudutāya  tajjassa ayonisomanasikārassa anibaddhabhāvato  vipallāsānaṃ tappaccayānañca mohamānādīnaṃ mudutarabhāvato  vatthupaṭisevanatoti adhippāyo tenāha tiādi
ti paṭisandhivasena sakiṃyeva āgamanasabhāvo ti iminā pañcasu sakadāgāmīsu cattāro vajjetvā ekoyeva gahitoti dassento tiādimāha tattha yvāyaṃ pañcamako sakadāgāmī idha maggaṃ bhāvetvā devaloke nibbatto tattha yāvatāyukaṃ ṭhatvā puna idhūpapajjitvā parinibbāyatīti vutto tassa ekabījinā saddhiṃ kiṃ nānākaraṇanti ekabījissa ekā paṭisandhi sakadāgāmissa dve paṭisandhiyoti idaṃ tesaṃ nānākaraṇaṃ yassa hi sotāpannassa ekaṃyeva khandhabījaṃ na ekaṃ attabhāvaggahaṇaṃ so ekabījīti
ti  amahaggatabhūmiyanti heṭṭhā sambandhanena heṭṭhābhāgassa hitāti  tesaṃ  orabbhāgiyasaṃyojanāni  ajjhattaṃ saṃyojanattā tathā hesa dūratopi āvattidhammo evāti dassetuṃ gilabaḷisamacchādayo upamābhāvena vuttā ti iminā gabbhavāsadukkhābhāvamāha ti iminā sesadukkhābhāvaṃ tattha parinibbānatā cassa kāmaloke khandhabījassa apunārohavasenevāti dassetuṃ ti vuttaṃ
ti lokiyābhiññāhi asammissā  tadavinābhāvato tāpi dassetuṃ ākaṅkheyya ce evamādimāhāti yojanā āsavānaṃ anavasesappahānato arahattamaggoyeva visesato āsavakkhayoti vattabbataṃ arahatīti vuttaṃ ti aññathā sabbāpi chaḷabhiññā āsavakkhayo evāti nti lokiyābhiññānaṃ  yathā purisassa muṇḍitaṃ sīsaṃ sikhāvirahitattā na sobhati evaṃ desanāya sīsabhūtāpi aggamaggakathā lokiyābhiññārahitā na sobhatīti āha ti ti iddhi ca vikubbanā ca vikubbanaggahaṇena cettha vikubbaniddhimāha iddhiggahaṇena tadaññaṃ sabbañca abhiññākiccaṃ ti lokiyābhiññānaṃ nibbattanassa viya desanāya yuttaṭṭhāneyeva etena na kevalaṃ desanakkamenevāyaṃ desanā atha kho paṭipattikkamenapīti dasseti    tasmā tattha vuttanayeneva veditabbāti adhippāyo
ti heṭṭhimamaggena khepitāvasiṭṭhānaṃ āsavānaṃ arahattamaggena samucchindanato yasmā arahattamaggo na kevalaṃ āsaveyeva khepeti atha kho avasiṭṭhe sabbakilesepi tasmā āha ti lakkhaṇamattañhettha āsavaggahaṇaṃ āsavānaṃ ārammaṇabhāvassapi anupagamanato anāsavaṃ yasmā pana tattha āsavānaṃ lesopi natthi tasmā vuttaṃ nti  cetosīsena yathā cittaṃ paññañca bhāvayanti  adhippāyo ti idaṃ ujuvipaccanīkapaṭippassaddhidassanaṃ daṭṭhabbaṃ na tadaññesaṃ pāpadhammānaṃ appaṭippassaddhattā idāni tameva samādhipaññānaṃ rāgāvijjāpaṭipakkhataṃ āgamena dassetuṃ ntiādi vuttaṃ nti samathassa phalaṃ lokiyasamathabhāvanāya hi vipassanāgatāya āhitaphalassa lokuttarasamathassa sarikkhakaphalo  nti etthāpi eseva nayo ti sutamayañāṇādinā viya parapaccayataṃ  nayaggāhañca muñcitvā paratoghosānugatabhāvanādhigamabhūtatāya attanoyeva  sayambhuñāṇabhūtāyāti adhippāyo tenāha ti
nti sabbampi sattarasavidhaṃ taṃ yathāvuttaṃ sīlānisaṃsaṃ yathā ānisaṃsavante sammadeva sampādite tadānisaṃsā dassitā eva honti tadāyattabhāvato evaṃ ānisaṃsapadhānayogyabhāvena dassite  tadānisaṃsā dassitā eva hontīti āha ti vuttasseva atthassa punavacanaṃ nigamananti vuttaṃ ti ti desanārambhe nti sampannasīlāti evamādinā ākārena vuttaṃ ti idaṃ sampannasīlātiādikaṃ sabbampi vacanaṃ ti etaṃ sampannasīlassa bhikkhuno yathāvuttasattarasavidhānisaṃsabhāgitaṃ sandhāya vuttaṃ idameva hi iti yaṃ taṃ vuttaṃ idametaṃ paṭicca vuttanti vacanaṃ sandhāya ti vuttaṃ etthaādito chahi ānisaṃsehi parittabhūmikā sampatti gahitā tadantaraṃ pañcahi lokiyābhiññāhi ca mahaggatabhūmikā itarehi lokuttarabhūmikāti evaṃ catubhūmikasampadānisaṃsasīlaṃ nāmetaṃ mahantaṃ mahānubhāvaṃ tasmā taṃsampādane sakkaccakāritā appamattena bhavitabbaṃ


 chādetabbaṃ  ṭhānaṃ vasati paṭicchādetīti  yaṃ samānaṃ viya na sabbaso minoti mānassa pana samīpe taṃ upamānaṃ upamīyati etāyāti upamā upamāya bodhakavacanaṃ   sutte nti upamiyatthaṃ paṭhamaṃ upamaṃ vatvā tadanantaraṃ atthaṃ vatvā puna upamaṃ vadanto ti vutto ti etthāpi eseva nayo idāni te cattāropi pakāre sutte āgatanayeneva dassento tiādimāha tattha ti dve paṭivissakagharā ti sammukhadvārā
nti so ayaṃ evaṃ upamādassanavasenapi nānānayenapi dhammadesako bhagavā ekaccānaṃ veneyyānaṃ atthassa sukhāvabodho paṭhamaṃ upamādassane hetu evaṃ paṭhamaṃ atthadassane upamāya atthaparivāraṇe atthena upamāparivāraṇe cāti imamatthaṃ dasseti ti  iminā ti sabbaññutaññāṇassa tañhi dhammadhātupariyāpannattā yathāvuttadhamme ca sabbepi ñeyyadhamme ca padahati yathāsabhāvato bujjhati bodheti cāti dhātu dhīyanti vā dhammā etāya sabbākārato ñāyanti ñāpiyanti cāti dhammadhātu tassā pana suṭṭhu saccasampaṭivedhavasena laddhattā ti yadaggena vā ñeyyaṃ tāya suppaṭividdhaṃ tadaggena sāpissa suppaṭividdhā evāti āha ti
pakatipariyodātassa cittassa āgantukehi upakkilesehi upakkiliṭṭhabhāvadassanatthaṃ saṃkiliṭṭhavatthadassananti katvā vuttaṃ nti ti ettharajo nāma reṇu -saddena aṇutajjāridhūmādikaṃ vatthassa aparisuddhikāraṇaṃ saṅgaṇhāti sabbaso kilissati vinassati visuddhi etenāti saṃkileso tena  vaṇṇavināsanena vidūsitaṃ  masi  vuccati loṇapaṭalādi chaviyā upari ṭhitaṃ sarīramalaṃ saddena sarīrajallameva assukheḷasiṅghāṇikādikaṃ tadaññamalaṃ saṅgaṇhāti ti pariyonandhanavasena gahitattā rajanti sattā tenāti raṅgaṃ raṅgameva  yathā kopameva kopajātaṃ ti pakkhipeyya ti nīlavaṇṇatthāya -saddena kāḷasāmādiṃ saṅgaṇhāti haliddikakudhaselādike  lākhāpattaṅgarasādike  mahārajanaloddakandulādike  duṭṭhu rajitavaṇṇaṃ apabhassaraṃ tenāha ti nti durattavaṇṇaṃ tasmiṃ vatthe raṅgajātaṃ sayaṃ suparisuddhaṃ samānaṃ kissa hetu kena rattavaṇṇaṃ aparisuddhaṃ hotīti raṅgajātassa niddosataṃ vadati tenāha tiādi
saṃkilesapakkhaṃ dassentena asaṃkiliṭṭhameva vatthaṃ udāharitabbanti pākaṭoyamattho saṃkiliṭṭhavatthanidassanena pana siyā nu kho aññopi koci visesoti adhippāyena pucchati tiādinā itaro atthavisesoti dassento ntiādimāha ettha ca saṃkiliṭṭhacittavisodhanavidhāne saṃkiliṭṭhavatthaṃ nidassatabbanti paṭiññā vāyāmamahapphaladassanatthanti hetuattho tiādi anvayattho tiādi byatirekattho sadisūdāharaṇaṃ pana malaggahitakaṃsapātiādi daṭṭhabbaṃ tiādi  opammatthassa upameyyaupanayanaṃ tattha ti akittimena sabhāvena tanti cittaṃ sāmaññaggahaṇañcetaṃ cittabhāvāvisesato tenāha ti  na saṃkiliṭṭhaṃ saṃkilesehi asamannāgatabhāvato nanu kiriyāmayacittehi vipākasantāne visesādhānaṃ labbhati aññathā katavināsā katabbhāgamā āpajjeyyuṃ kiñcāpi labbhati tassa saṃkileso vaṭṭupanissayo asuddhi vā na hoti asaṃkileso vivaṭṭupanissayo visuddhi vā na hoti eva nti panetaṃ upakkilesanārahassa cittassa vasena vuttaṃ na vipākapabandhassa tenāha nti ti ca ti pana sakasantatipariyāpannatāya nesaṃ kevalaṃ ekattanayavasena vuttaṃ na vipākadhammānaṃ kilesāsamaṅgibhāvato atha vā nti iminā upakkilesahetu tattha vijjamānaṃ visesādhānamāha na saṃkiliṭṭhā dhammātiādīsu  viya taṃsamaṅgitanti daṭṭhabbaṃ nti vipassanāpaññāya anukkamena sabbupakkilesehi vimociyamānaṃ  aggamaggakkhaṇe  yato na puna upakkilissati ntiādi vuttassevatthassa nigamanaṃ
duṭṭhagatiparipūraṇavasena paṭipajjanaṃ  sā eva kilesadarathapariḷāhādivasena upāyāsadukkhā kucchitā vā gati pavatti duggatihetūti vā  duggatiyā pana paṭipattiyā gandhabbato tassā vā nipphannabhāvato kucchito dukkhā ca gatīti  ti idaṃ tassā paṭipattiyā duggatibhāvadassanatthaṃ na visesanatthaṃ na hi asaṃkiliṭṭhacittassa pāṇaghātādivasena pavatti ti lābhāsāya sabbaso kiliṭṭhacitto  nti dūteyyaṃ vuccati dutakammaṃ gihīnaṃ paṇṇaṃ vā sāsanaṃ vā gahetvā tattha tattha gamanaṃ pahiṇagamanaṃ gharāgharaṃ pesitassa khuddakagamanaṃ dūteyyagamanaṃ pahiṇagamanañca gacchati nti ananuññāte ṭhāne lābhāsāya gahaṭṭhānaṃ bhesajjaṃ karoti kathā parato āgamissati ti veḷudānapattadānapupphadānādīhi micchājīvena  ti atthi anācāro atthi agocarotiādinā   āgataṃ sabbampi anācāraṃ agocarañca caraṇavasena paripūreti
ti vatvā tattha pettivisayagamanaṃ dassento tiādimāha
sukkapakkhe nti sabbaso visuddhaṃ asaṃkiliṭṭhaṃ parisuddhattā eva  pabhassaranti attho ti suṭṭhu rattavaṇṇameva assa ti nīlavaṇṇopissa parisuddho ca bhaveyyāti evamādiṃ sandhāyāha ti ntiādi pana tattha vuttavaseneva veditabbaṃ ādīsu yaṃ vattabbaṃ taṃ paṭipattiduggatiādīsu vuttavipariyāyena veditabbaṃ ti suddhāsayo ti idaṃ kaṇhapakkhe dasa akusalakammapathe paripūretīti vuttassa paṭipakkhadassanavasena vuttaṃ yathā hi tattha abhijjhābyāpādamicchādiṭṭhiggahaṇena kammapathasaṃsandananayena kammapathaṃ appattāya ca agāriyassa tathārūpāya micchāpaṭipattiyā saṅgaho icchito evaṃ idhāpi anabhijjhāabyāpādasammādiṭṭhiggahaṇena alobhādosāmohavasena pavattā agāriyassa sammāpaṭipatti saṅgahitāti daṭṭhabbaṃ na kammapathappattāvāti nti jātirūpabhogādhipateyyādivasena manussesu mahantabhāvaṃ dasahi ṭhānehi aññesaṃ devānaṃ abhibhavo  paṭipatti sugatiyā bhājiyamānattā ti tathā anāgāmibhāvanaṃ pāpetvā ṭhapitā gahitaggahaṇena sukhānubhavaṭṭhānassa adhippetattā tadabhāvato asaññibhavaṃ anādiyanto tiādimāha
 abhijjhāyanaṭṭhena  abhijjhāyanāti attho  visamaṃ lubbhatīti  evampi abhijjhāvisamalobhānaṃ viseso hotīti dassento tiādimāha tattha attano santakaṃ taṃsadisañca  yaṃ yācitaṃ appakasirena vā sakkā laddhuṃ taṃ  paradāragarudārāti  yaṃ apatthaniyaṃ yassa  vā patthanāya byasanaṃ āpajjati taṃ  ti  yena  potthakaṃ āropitā so hi antevāsikesu sākacchantesu evamāha sopi imasmiṃyeva sutte vinibbhogo na labbhati cittasaṃkilesassa adhippetattā tenāha tiādi ayonisomanasikāravasena  uppajjanato sampatti āyatiñca dukkhasseva uppādanato  ti yassa kassaci ārammaṇassa yuttassa ayuttassa appattassa ca abhijjāyanavasena abhipatthanāvasena ca pavattā taṇhā ti lobhato nibbisesanti dasseti tenāha nti ti sabhāvasantaṃ asaṃkilesaṃ vināseti avisuddhaṃ karoti tenāha ti ime sattā ucchijjantu vinassantūti sattesu byāpajjanākārappavattiyā  vutto kodho pana saṅkhāresupi pavattanato dasavidhaāghātavatthusambhavo vutto ubhayampi paṭighameva pavattanānattato bhinditvā vutto kujjhanavaseneva  akkocchi maṃ avadhi mantiādinā
suṭṭhu kataṃ karaṇaṃ  tassa pubbakāritālakkhaṇassa guṇassa  udakapuñchaniyā viya sarīrānugataṃ udakaṃ puñchanto  tathā hi so paresaṃ guṇānaṃ makkhanaṭṭhena makkhoti vuccati idāni tiādinā saṅkhepena vuttatthaṃ vitthārena dassetuṃ tiādi vuttaṃ nisinnakathāparikathādivasena dhammassa kathā dhammakathānayo ekattādidhammanīti eva vā pakaraṇaṃ satta pakaraṇāni tattha kosallaṃ  -saddena vinayakkame catūsu mahānikāyesu ca kosallaṃ saṅgaṇhāti ti cittīkārarahito nti iminā yathāyaṃ makkho cittaṃ dūseti evaṃ paḷāsopi cittaṃ dūseti tasmā upakkilesoti dasseti -saddena rattaññū cirapabbajite puggale ajjhottharitvā tvampi imasmiṃ sāsane pabbajito ahampi pabbajito tvampi sīlamatte ṭhito ahampīti evamādīnaṃ saṅgaho ti tava vā mama vā ko visesoti asamampi samaṃ katvā samadhuraggāhagaṇhanako  usūyanā attano sampattiyā nigūhanaṃ tassa parehi sādhāraṇabhāvāsahanena hotīti icceva vuttaṃ kāraṇe hi gahite phalampi gahitameva hotīti aññathā attano pavedanakapuggalo  nekatikavāṇijotipi vadanti sappamukhā  macchavālā ekā macchajāti āyatanamaccho tenāha tiādi ti antevāsī
sabbaso  amadditasabhāvena vā tabharitabhattasadisassa thaddhabhāvassa anonamitadaṇḍasadisatāya paggahitasiraanivātavuttikārassa ca karaṇato ti yaṃ yena kataṃ duccaritaṃ vā sucaritaṃ vā taduttari tassa dviguṇaṃ vā karaṇo attano maṇḍanādiatthaṃ   attano balānurūpaṃ kāmaṃ nikāyadvayaggahaṇādivasena pavatto sevitabbamāno eva tathāpissa saṃkilesapakkhattā vuttaṃ ti
ti seyyohamasmītiādinā cittassa paggahaṇavasena pubbe kenaci attānaṃ sadisaṃ katvā pacchā tato adhikato dahanato uppajjanako   jātiādiṃ paṭicca majjanākāro sopi atthato māno eva  tathāpavatto cittuppādo
ti lobhassa ādito gahaṇe kāraṇaṃ vibhāvetukāmo pucchati ti tattha tattha bhave sabbapaṭhamaṃ uppajjanato sattānañhi yathādhigataṃ jhānādivisesaṃ ārabbha paccavekkhaṇā viya yathāladdhaṃ upapatibhavaṃ ārabbha nikanti eva tenāha ntiādi ti itare byāpādādayo yathāpaccayaṃ uppajjanti lobhassa viya ādito asukassa anantaraṃ asukoti vā na nesaṃ niyamo atthīti attho kiṃ pana ete soḷaseva cittassa upakkilesā udāhu aññepi santīti anuyogaṃ sandhāya aññepi santīti dassento tiādimāha yadi evaṃ kasmā ettakā eva idha vuttāti nayadassanavasenāti dassento āha ti tena thinamiddhauddhaccakukkucca-vicikicchā-attukkaṃsana-paravabbhanachambhitattā- bhīrukatā-ahirikānottappa-atticchatā-pāpicchatā-mahicchatādayo saṅgahitāti veditabbaṃ
ti saṃkiliṭṭhavattanidassanena saṅkhepena vuttaṃ saṃkilesaṃ vibhāgena dassetvā ti etthāpi eseva nayo ti abhijjhā visamalobho ekanteneva cittassa uppakkilesoti sabhāvato samudayato nirodhato nirodhūpāyato ca pubbabhāgapaññāya ceva heṭṭhimamaggadvayapaññāya ca jānitvā ti ettha accantappahānameva adhippetanti dassento ti āha ti anāgāmimaggena tena hi pahānaṃ idha sabbavāresu adhippetaṃ  idha kilesānaṃ desanākkamo pana catunnaṃ ariyamaggānaṃ desanākkamopi tāya desanāya paṭipajjanakkamopi  tāya paṭipattiyā uppattikkamopi tattha ye ye kilesā yena yena maggena pahīyanti maggapaṭipāṭiṃ anoloketvā tesaṃ tesaṃ kilesānaṃ tena tena maggena pahānadassanaṃ kilesapaṭipāṭi na kilesānaṃ uppattikkamo idha desanākkamo cāti dassento tiādimāha yena yena pana maggena ye ye kilesā pahīyanti maggānupubbiyā tena tena maggena tesaṃ tesaṃ kilesānaṃ pahānadassanaṃ maggapaṭipāṭiyā pahānadassananti dassento tiādimāha
ti sa kho so bhikkhave bhikkhūtiādinā āgato imasmiṃ pahānavāre ti ime yathāvuttā kilesā heṭṭhā dassitamaggapaṭipāṭivasena tattha pana ye tatiyamaggavajjhā tesaṃ anāgāmimaggeneva pahāne vattabbaṃ natthi yesaṃ panettha heṭṭhimamaggavajjhānaṃ idha saṅgahe kāraṇaṃ pacchā vattukāmena aggamaggavajjhānaṃ anādiyitvā kasmā tatiyamaggavajjhānameva gahaṇaṃ katanti āha ti ayaṃ imassa suttassa etasmiṃ ṭhāne ācariyapaveṇiyā kathāmaggo tato āgato atthasambhavo atthatatvanti attho tattha heṭṭhimamaggavajjhānaṃ idha saṅgahe kāraṇaṃ pacchā vattukāmo aggamaggavajjhānaṃ aggahaṇe yuttiṃ dassento tiādimāha ti catutthamaggena nti byāpādādīnaṃ  ti makkhādike sandhāyāha nti tesaṃ makkhādīnaṃ samuṭṭhāpakacittuppādānaṃ tattha makkha-paḷāsa-issā-macchariya-samuṭṭhāpakaṃ paṭighadvayacittaṃ visesato pañcakāmaguṇalobhena saṭho māyāvī ca hoti pañcakāmaguṇikarāgo ca anāgāmimaggeneva niravasesato pahīyati tasmā vuttaṃ ti tepi suppahīnā hontīti sambandho nti paṭhamamaggeneva pahānaṃ  yathodhi khoti ettha odhivacanassa maggattayavācakattā ratanattaye aveccappasādo nāma ariyakantasīlaṃ viya sotāpannassa aṅgāni te ca pahānato pacchā niddiṭṭhā tasmā idha vuttappahānaṃ vikkhambhanapahānamevāti keci vadanti  yathāvuttapahānasseva vasena aveccappasādānaṃ odhiso pahānassa vibhāvitattā svāyamattho heṭṭhā yuttitopi pakāsitoyeva
 yato ekamekassapi upakkilesassa sabhāvādito dassanaṃ niyyānamukhaṃ hoti tathā ceva heṭṭhā saṃvaṇṇitaṃ anāgāmimaggavasena pahānaṃ vatvā pasādassa uddhaṭattā vuttaṃ ti yadi evaṃ kasmā lokiyo uppajjatīti vuttanti itipi so bhagavātiādinayappavattassa lokiyattā nibbānārammaṇo  eva hi lokuttaro pasādo itipi so bhagavātiādivacanena lokiyaṃ aveccappasādavacanena lokuttaranti  avecca ratanattayaguṇe yāthāvato ñatvā pasādo  so pana yasmā maggenāgatattā kenaci akampaniyo appadhaṃsiyo ca hoti tasmā vuttaṃ ti tattha lokuttaro sabbaso buddhaguṇādīsu sammohaṃ viddhaṃsento tattha kiccato pavattati itaro ārammaṇavasena te ārabbha nti taṃ tassa uppannappakāraṃ ti anussatikammaṭṭhānāni
ti -saddena ñāṇādīni saṅgaṇhāti corānaṃ abhiṇhaṃ sañcaraṇaṭṭhānatāya ggahaṇaṃ ti asukasmiñca ṭhāne ime cime corā evañca evañca vināsitāti paccavekkhato 
yo  yo odhi  yathā-saddo byāpanicchāyaṃ kho saddo avadhāraṇeti dassento tiādimāha tena vantantiādīsupi avadhāretabbanti dasseti ti saṅkhepato vuttamatthaṃ vivarituṃ tiādi āraddhaṃ tattha ti yena maggena anavasesato pahātabbā anavasesappahānavasena hi taṃtaṃmaggavajjhānaṃ kilesānaṃ tadaññamaggavajjhehi asammissatā aññathā ye sakasakaodhivasena uparimaggavajjhā te heṭṭhimamaggehi pahīnāpāyagamanīyādisabhāvā eva tehi pahīyantīti pahānavasena sammissā siyuṃ ti etthāpi eseva nayo ti tato pahānanimittasomanassuppattito uddhampi paṭipakkhesu odhiso pavattikiccattā  tiādi vuttassevatthassa vivaraṇaṃ ti anāgāmiṃ sandhāyāha tena vuttaṃ nti
keci cattampi gaṇhanti nayidamevanti dassanatthaṃ nti vuttaṃ na hi yaṃ yena vantaṃ so puna taṃ ādiyati tenāha ti vantampi kiñci sasantatilaggaṃ siyā nayidamevanti dassanatthaṃ nti vuttaṃ tenāha ti muttampi kiñci muttabandhanā viya phalaṃ kuhiñci tiṭṭhati na evamidanti dassanatthaṃ nti vuttaṃ tenāha ti yathā kiñci dunnissaṭṭhaṃ puna ādāya sammadeva nissaṭṭhaṃ paṭinissaṭṭhanti vuccati evaṃ vipassanāya nissaṭṭhaṃ ādinnasadisaṃ maggena pahīnaṃ paṭinissaṭṭhaṃ nāma hotīti dassanatthaṃ nti vuttaṃ tenāha ti na kāpurisena viya parammukhena nissaṭṭhaṃ  atha kho abhimukheneva nissaṭṭhanti dassanatthaṃ nti vuttaṃ tenāha tiādi ti attano hitasukhaṃ paccāsīsantena ekantena adhigantabbato ti taṃsamaṅgīnaṃ apāyapātato sandhāraṇena  vidanti etenāti vedehi ñāṇehi gato paṭipannoti  ti jāneyya ti uppannasomanassā  veditabbaṃ vedetīti  ārammaṇarasaṃ vindati anubhavatīti
nti  aveccappasādaṃ nissāya uppannaṃ nti somanassaṃ somanassamayañāṇañcāti evaṃ vuttappakārameva nti atthe hetuphale vedaṃ nti dhamme hetumhi vedaṃ tenāha ntiādi idha dhammatthasaddā hetuphalapariyāyāti imamatthaṃ pāḷiyā eva dassetuṃ ntiādi vuttaṃ ti attho dhammoti ca vuttaṃ aveccappasādanimittaṃ yathāvuttaṃ kilesappahānañca nti yathāvuttaatthadhammānisaṃsabhūtaṃ somanassamayañāṇasaṅkhātaṃ vedañca nti taruṇapītiṃ āha ti etena paccavekkhaṇā evettha anavajjasabhāvatāya dhammoti vuttoti daṭṭhabbaṃ ti parappaccayaṃ balavapītimāha ti passaddhiāvahehi uḷārehi pītivegehi tittacittassa ti nāmakāyo ti kilesapariḷāhānaṃ dūrībhāvena suṭṭhu upasantadaratho paccavekkhaṇahetukaṃ cittassa samādhānaṃ idha adhippetanti āha ti
 kāmaṃ buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgatomhi dhamme saṅghe aveccappasādena samannāgatomhīti idampi tassā paccavekkhaṇāya pavattiākārapakāsanameva idaṃ pana visesato ratanattaye uppannasomanassādippakāsanapadaṃ yathodhi kho panāti idampi savisesaṃ paccavekkhaṇākārappakāsanapadanti adhippāyena ti vuttaṃ cattāropi pana vārā paccavekkhaṇākārappakāsanavasena ceva somanassādiānisaṃsadassanavasena ca vuttāti sakkā viññātuṃ ubhayatthāpi ubhayassa vuttattā yadipi ariyamaggo ekacittakkhaṇiko na puna uppajjati paṭipakkhassa pana tena suppahīnattā taṃsamaṅgī aparihānadhammo taṃsīlādibhāveneva vuccatīti āha tiādi evaṃdhammā te bhagavanto ahesuntiādīsu  viya idha dhamma-saddo samādhipariyāyoti āha ti tathā hi so sampayuttadhamme ekārammaṇe avikkhipamāne  avippakiṇṇe avisaṭe katvā samaṃ sammā ca ādahanto tathā te dhāretīti ca vattabbataṃ arahatīti  dhammoti ca vuccati nti anekappakārānaṃ antarāyo nāma appaṭiladdhassa vā alabbhanavasena paṭiladdhassa vā parihānavasena tadubhayampi idha natthīti dassento tiādimāha ti tassa anāgāmino piṇḍapātabhojanaṃ neva hoti antarāyāya ukkaṃsagatāya paccavekkhaṇāya paccavekkhitvā paribhuñjanato tañcassā ukkaṃsagamanaṃ hatapaṭipakkhattāti dassento ti āha
ti etasmiṃ antarāyābhāve  visuddhacittattameva  ettha ca nevassa taṃ hoti antarāyāyāti iminā heṭṭhā vuttappahānaṃ anāgāmimaggenevāti siddhaṃ hoti anāgāmino hi sabbaso kāmarāgo pahīno hoti rasataṇhāya abhāvato tādisapiṇḍapātaparibhogo aggamaggādhigame kathañcipi antarāyāya na hotīti seyyathāpi bhikkhave vatthanti vadanto bhagavāādimhi attanā upanītavatthūpamaṃ anusandheti udakassa acchabhāvo paṅkasevālapaṇakādimalābhāvena pasannatāya tabbipariyāyato bahalatāti āha nti vaṇṇanibhāya vigatasaṃkilesatāya samujjalanaṃ pabhassaratāya vatthassa taṃ pariyodātanti vattabbataṃ labhatīti āha ti ti aṅgārakapallaṃ yathā dārughaṭikaṅgārādikena na bhijjati evaṃ tanumattikālepādinā bandheyya meghapaṭalato verambhavātadhārāsaṅghaṭṭanato vijjutā viya kevalaṃ vātadhārāsaṅghaṭṭanajanitā pabhā ukkāpabhā sā pana yasmā dvinnaṃ vātadhārānaṃ vegasambhūtasaṅghaṭṭanahetukā tasmā kāraṇavasena ti vuttaṃ
tiādimhi uṭṭhitadesanāya anurūpā anusandhi yathānusandhi tassā vasena byatirekadassanaṃ viya hi sādhetabbassa ādimhi uṭṭhitadesanāya paṭipakkhadassanampi anurūpadesanāva sammadeva patiṭṭhāpanabhāvato yathā taṃ āvattahārayojanāyaṃ visabhāgadhammāvattanti daṭṭhabbaṃ ti saṅkhepato vuttamatthaṃ vitthārento tappasaṅgena itarepi anusandhī dassetuṃ tiādimāha ti bāhiresu vatthūsu ti taṇhādiṭṭhiparitassanābhāvo ti idha bhikkhu ekaccassātiādinā   vissajjitasuttavasena ti sīlādivodānadhammesu akkhantiyādisaṃkilesadhammesu ca yena yena dhammena ti iminā anurūpadhammavasena vāti vuttavikappaṃ dasseti sesehi paṭipakkhavasena vāti  vuttavikappaṃ akkhantiyā hi kakacūpamovādo  paṭipakkho tathā diṭṭhiyā netaṃ mama nesohamasmi na meso attāti evaṃ paṭibhāgā suññatākārena sesadvayepi eseva nayo citte saṃkiliṭṭhe duggati pāṭikaṅkhāti  heṭṭhā kilesadesanā āgatā ti anavaseso ti ādīnavānisaṃsapaccavekkhaṇapuggaladosajānanādinā sabbappakārena
 mettā bhāvetabbā byāpādassa pahānāyātiādivacanato  mettādayo byāpādavihesāratirāgānaṃ paṭipakkhā yasmā so atthītiādinā bhagavatā anāgāmino aggamaggādhigamanaṃ catusaccakammaṭṭhānaṃ matthakaṃ pāpetvā kathitaṃ tasmā taṃ dassento tiādimāha
ti brahmavihāre ceva brahmavihārasahagatadhamme ca tenāha ti vavatthapetvāti ānetvā sambandhitabbaṃ nāmantipi hi īdisesu ṭhānesu cattāro arūpino khandhā vuccanti ti etena bhūtanissitānaṃ sesupādāyadhammānaṃ sabbesampi pahātabbataṇhāvajjānaṃ tebhūmakadhammānaṃ pariggahavidhiṃ ulliṅgeti sabhāvato vijjamānaṃ taṃ attapaccakkhaṃ katvā ñāṇena yāthāvato paṭivijjhiyamānataṃ upādāya atthi idanti yathāvavatthāpitaṃ nāmarūpaṃ tenevāha ti sāvadhāraṇañcetaṃ vacanaṃ lokasamaññāsiddhaṃ sattaitthipurisādi viya ito bāhirakaparikappitaṃ pakatiādi drabyādi jīvādi kāyādi viya ca na paramatthato natthi atthevāti vuttaṃ hoti ti pubbabhāge tāva lakkhaṇarasādivasena ceva paṭiggahavibhāgavasena ca pakārato jānāti aparabhāge pana pariññābhisamayavasena paṭivijjhanto jānāti ekantahīnā nāma akusaladhammā sampati āyatiñca dukkhamūlattā tatthāpi visesato taṇhāti āha ti attano paccayehi padhānabhāvaṃ nītattā paṇītanti iminā atthena ariyamaggova paṇītanti vuccatīti āha ti uttamaṭṭhena ca paṇītanti vuccamāne nirodhasaccassapi saṅgaho siyā tassa pana padantarena saṅgahitattā vuttanayenevettha attho veditabbo appamaññāmukhena vipassanābhinivesasseva katattā ti vuttaṃ sabbassapi tebhūmakassa saññāgatassāti vattuṃ vaṭṭatiyeva na cettha asaṅgaho tassāpi saññāya āgatabhāvato lokaṃ uttaritvā samatikkamitvā nissaritvā visaṃyuttaṃ hutvā ṭhitattā vuttaṃ nti
ti atthi hīnantiādīhi catūhi pakārehi anvayañāṇatāya anubodhabhūtāya vipassanāpaññāya jānanattho dhammañāṇatāya paṭivedhabhūtāya maggapaññāya dassanattho sabhāvasiddhoti dassento ti vuttaṃ ti bhayabheravasuttavaṇṇanāyaṃ attanā vuttaatthavacanatthapāṭhena idha pāṭhassa sadisattā atidisanto ti āha ettha ca yasmā kāmāsavāpi cittaṃ vimuccati avijjāsavāpi cittaṃ vimuccatīti khīṇā jātītiādīni vadatā bhagavatā catutthamaggo niddiṭṭho tasmā yaṃ heṭṭhā  vuttaṃ so ca upari catutthamaggasseva niddiṭṭhattā yujjatīti taṃ suvuttamevāti daṭṭhabbaṃ
ti tassa brāhmaṇassa bhagavā attano codanatthāya puccha maṃ tvaṃ brāhmaṇa yadettha tayā manasābhisamīhitanti codanāya okāsadānatthāyāti adhippāyo desanāsannissayo brāhmaṇassa tathārūpo ettha ajjhāsayopi natthīti yathāvuttaanusandhittayavinimuttattā ti vuttaṃ cittagatattā  ti kilesamalapavāhanena rāgapariḷāhādivūpasamakarena ca aṭṭhaṅgikaariyamaggasalilasinānena
 dhammasabhāmaṇḍapaṃ tāvadeva upagatattā bāhukā nadito  ariyaphalamaddanacuṇṇādayo telasinehassa vivecanena  lūkhabhāvo lokaṃ taṃ etissā atthīti lokāti sammatā ggahaṇena tathā sā nadī loke pākaṭāti evaṃ pavattaṃ attano micchāgāhaṃ dīpeti tenāha ti pāpapavāhanena samparāyikādisampattiāvahato lokassa hitā  lokyāti sammatāti sabbaṃ purimasadisaṃ tenāha ti ti pujjabhavaphalanibbattanena sattānaṃ punanena visodhanena puññāti sammatā ti tassā pubbe āgatadesanāya atthadīpanatthameva vuttassevatthassa puna dīpanaṃ kimatthiyanti āha nti cuṇṇikavacanaṃ asambhāventā tathā ca vutte atthamabujjhanakā pajjavacanaṃ sambhāventā tathā ca vutte bujjhanakā gāthārucikā nti visiṭṭhadīpanatthaṃ purimadesanāya aññadīpanatthanti attho
gacchati pana bhavaṃ gotamo bāhukaṃ nadiṃ sināyitunti  heṭṭhā vuttattā   adhikakkādivacanāni tato visiṭṭhassa atthassa bodhanato  kasmā panettha bhagavatā brāhmaṇena avuttāni adhikakkādīni gahitānīti āha tiādi kakkanti nhānapiṇḍaṃ adhippetaṃ nhāyitvā adhikaṃ kakkaṃ ettha gaṇhantīti  tenāha tiādi nti vaṭṭapokkharaṇīsaṇṭhānaṃ ti visuṃ nadiyo na adhikakkādīni viya titthamattaṃ
